       function SerachByPatientNo()
   {
       try
       {
           if (!$("#txtPatientNo").validate(MSG_INFO)) return;
           var patMrNo = $("#txtPatientId").getValue();
           var mobileNo = $("#txtPatientNo").getValue();
           if (mobileNo == "____-_______")
               return;
           if (mobileNo == "") {
               return
           }
           if (mobileNo != "" || mobileNo != undefined) {
               $("#loading-image").show();
               var _url = '@Url.Action("GetPatientBySearch", "InsuranceInvoice")';
               var data = JSON.stringify({ keyWord: mobileNo });
               $.AjaxJsonAsynRequest(_url, data, function (msg) {
                   if (msg.lstPatient != null) {

                       if (msg.lstPatient.length > 0) {
                           //Clear();
                           $("#modalboxPatient").show("modal");
                           Fill_PatientPopUp(msg.lstPatient);
                           $("#loading-image").hide();
                       }
                       else {
                           $("#modalboxPatient").hide("modal");
                           $("#loading-image").hide();
                       }
                   }
                   else {
                       ShowMessage(1, "No Record Found");
                       $("#loading-image").hide();
                   }
               });
           }
       } catch (e) {

       }
   }

    function CheckDOB(flag, val) {
        try {
            if (flag == "M") {
                if (new Number(val) > 12) {
                    ShowMessage('1', 'Month should be less than or equal to 12');
                    $("#txtMonth").val("0");
                    return;
                }
            }
            else if (flag == "D") {
                if (new Number(val) > 31) {
                    ShowMessage('1', 'Days should be less than or equal to 31');
                    $("#txtDay").val("0");
                    return;
                }
            }

        } catch (e) {
            console.log(e.message);
        }
    }


            function FillProOrderCPCTable(obj) {
                debugger;
                isCheckZero = true;
                ClearGrid($("#tblProOrderCPC tr").length, "trProOrderCPC");

                if (obj.length == 0) {
                    $("#ddl_PatientCategory").enable();
                    $("#txtProTotalAmount").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtProDiscountNet").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtProDiscountPer").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtProPayableAmount").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtProPaidAmount").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtProBalance").setValue(0);
                    return;

                var cols = Object.getOwnPropertyNames(obj[0]).sort();

                        deptLst = obj[i].DepartmentId.split(',').map(Number);

                            // Check 1: Exact match with DepartmentId, SectionId, and ServiceId
                            for (let k = 0; k < deptLst.length; k++) {
                                if (
                                    lstOfCopayDetail[j].DepartmentId == deptLst[k] &&
                                    lstOfCopayDetail[j].SectionId == obj[i].SectionId &&
                                    lstOfCopayDetail[j].ServiceId == obj[i].ServiceId
                                ) {
                                    CopayPer = lstOfCopayDetail[j].Copay;
                                    isFounded = true;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }

                            // Check 2: Match DepartmentId and SectionId
                            if (!isFounded) {
                                for (let k = 0; k < deptLst.length; k++) {
                                    if (
                                        lstOfCopayDetail[j].DepartmentId == deptLst[k] &&
                                        lstOfCopayDetail[j].SectionId == obj[i].SectionId
                                    ) {
                                        CopayPer = lstOfCopayDetail[j].Copay;
                                        isFounded = true;
                                        break;
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            // Check 3: Match DepartmentId only
                            if (!isFounded) {
                                for (let k = 0; k < deptLst.length; k++) {
                                    if (lstOfCopayDetail[j].DepartmentId == deptLst[k]) {
                                        CopayPer = lstOfCopayDetail[j].Copay;
                                        isFounded = true;
                                        break;
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            if (isFounded) {
                                break; // Stop looping once found
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    let Copay = 0;

                    if (!isNaN(CopayPer) && CopayPer > 0) {
                        Copay = (Inusranceprice / 100) * CopayPer;
                        Copay = Copay.toFixed(2);
                    } else {
                        Copay = 0; // fallback value or you can set to null or a default percentage
                    }

                    var CopayPercentage = "";
                    //if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_APPROVED || obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_REJECTED) {

                    var CopayPrice = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +

    function updateProQuantity(i) {
                var quantityValue = $("#txtProQuantity" + i).val();
                quantityValue = Math.max(1, parseInt(quantityValue, 10));
                selectedProcCPTs[i].Quantity = quantityValue;

                console.log("Updated Quantity for Service ID " + selectedProcCPTs[i].ServiceId + ": " + selectedProcCPTs[i].Quantity);
            }





    function DeleteProCPCOrderGrid(index) {


        debugger;
        if ($("#txtReceiptVoucherId").getValue() != "") {
            var getServicePrice = new Number($("#txtProModePrice" + selectedProcCPTs[index].ServiceId + "_" + index).getValue());
            var balanceAmount = new Number($("#txtProBalance").getValue());
            var disc = new Number($("#txtProDiscountPer").getValue());
            var disAmount = Math.round((getServicePrice / 100) * disc);
            getServicePrice = getServicePrice - disAmount;
            //var remainingAmount = payAbleAmount - getServicePrice;
            // var totalRecieved = new Number($("#txtProPaidAmount").getValue());
            //if (remainingAmount < totalRecieved) {
            if (balanceAmount < getServicePrice) {
                ShowMessage('1', 'can not be delete this record,please refund.');
                return;
            }
        }


        isEdit = false;
        var GrandTotal = 0;
        //////////////
        if (selectedProcCPTs[index].Price != undefined) {
            GrandTotal = new Number(ProTotalAmount) - selectedProcCPTs[index].Price;
        }

        selectedProcCPTs.splice(index, 1);
        GrandTotal = GetProTotalPrice();

        FillProOrderCPCTable(selectedProcCPTs);

        if (GrandTotal != 0) {
            ProTotalAmount = GrandTotal;

            $("#txtProTotalAmount").setValue(GrandTotal);

            $("#txtTotalPro").empty();
            $("#txtTotalPro").append("Total Price = " + GrandTotal + "\tPKR");
            $("#txtTotalProTest").empty();
            $("#txtTotalProTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedProcCPTs.length + "");
            $("#txtProDiscountNet").trigger("onchange");
        }
        else {
            if (selectedProcCPTs.length == 0) {
                ProTotalAmount = GrandTotal;


                $("#txtProTotalAmount").setValue(GrandTotal);

                $("#txtTotalPro").empty();
                $("#txtTotalPro").append("Total Price = " + GrandTotal + "\tPKR");
                $("#txtTotalProTest").empty();
                $("#txtTotalProTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedProcCPTs.length + "");
                $("#txtProDiscountNet").trigger("onchange");
            }
        }
        $("#txtTotalProTest").empty();
        $("#txtTotalProTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedProcCPTs.length + "");

        $("#txtProRefundBalance").setValue(0);
        @*if ('@ViewBag.IsRecieveAmount' == 'False' || $("#txtPatientAdmitId").getValue() != "")
            $("#txtProPaidAmount").setValue(0);*@
    }



    var isEdit = false;
    function GetLabOrderData(Id) {
        var patientOrder = new Array();
        $("#loading-image").show();
        var _url = '@Url.Action("GetLabOrderData", "InsuranceInvoice")';
        var _data = "{id:'" + Id + "'}";
        $.AjaxJsonAsynRequest(_url, _data, function (msg) {

            debugger;
            if (msg != null) {

                debugger
                patientOrder = $.parseJSON(msg);


                var e = jQuery.Event("keypress");
                e.keyCode = $.ui.keyCode.ENTER;
                Search(e.keyCode, patientOrder[0].PatientId);
                debugger
                var d = new Date(patientOrder[0].DOB);
                var dt = ('0' + d.getDate()).slice(-2) + "/" + ('0' + (d.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "/" + d.getFullYear();
                $('#dpkDOB').val(dt);
                CalculateAge();

                if (patientOrder[0].DepartmentId != null) {
                    $("#txtDepartmentId").val(patientOrder[0].DepartmentId);
                }
                var d = new Date(patientOrder[0].PatientOrderOn);
                var dt = ('0' + (d.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "/" + ('0' + d.getDate()).slice(-2) + "/" + d.getFullYear();
                $('#dpkPatientOrderOn').val(dt);

                $("#txtPatientAdmitId").setValue(patientOrder[0].PatientAdmitId);
                $("#txtPatientRequisitionId").setValue(patientOrder[0].PatientRequisitionId);

                $("#txtDepartmentComponentId").setValue(patientOrder[0].DepartmentComponentId);
                $("#txtParentPatientOrderId").setValue(patientOrder[0].ParentPatientOrderId);


                $("#txtPatientVisitId").setValue(patientOrder[0].PatientVisitId);


                $("#txtProDiscountNet").setValue(patientOrder[0].TotalDiscount);
                $("#txtProDiscountPer").setValue(patientOrder[0].DiscPercent);
                $("#ddl_LabPaymode").setValue(patientOrder[0].PaymentMethodProfileId);

                $("#txtProCashReceived").setValue(Math.floor(patientOrder[0].CashReceived));
                $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").setValue(Math.floor(patientOrder[0].CreditCardReceived));
                $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").setValue(Math.floor(patientOrder[0].PatientAccountReceived));
                $("#txtProReturn").setValue(patientOrder[0].TotalReturnAmount);
                if ('@ViewBag.DocMovementShortName' != "CLNPOD") {
                    $("#txtConsultant").setValue(patientOrder[0].EmployeeName);
                    $("#txtConsultant").disable();
                }
                selectedProcCPTs = patientOrder;
                FillProOrderCPCTable(selectedProcCPTs);


                $("#txtProPatientOrderSetId").setValue(patientOrder[0].PatientOrderSetId);
                $("#ddl_PatientCategory").setValue(patientOrder[0].BillCategoryProfileId);



                if (patientOrder[0].OrderRemarks != null) {
                    $("#txtRemarks").setValue(patientOrder[0].OrderRemarks);
                }


                $("#txtInvoiceId").setValue(patientOrder[0].InvoiceId);

                $("#txtReceiptVoucherId").setValue(patientOrder[0].ReceiptVoucherId);
                $("#txtVoucherId").setValue(patientOrder[0].VoucherId);
                isEdit = true;









            }
        });
    }

    $(window).bind("load", function () {
        $("#txtProCurrentAmount").trigger("onkeyup");
    });

    function GetInsuranceApprovelData(Id) {
 debugger

        $("#loading-image").show();

        let docMovementShortName = '@ViewBag.DocMovementShortName';
        var _url = '@Url.Action("GetInsuranceApprovelData", "InsuranceInvoice")';
        var _data = "{id:'" + Id + "',shortName:'" + docMovementShortName + "'}";
        //var _data = "{id:'" + Id + "'}";
        $.AjaxJsonAsynRequest(_url, _data, function (msg) {
            debugger
            if (msg.insuranceStatus != null) {

                console.log(msg.insuranceStatus.FilePath);
                if (msg.insuranceStatus.FilePath !=null) {
                    $("#InusranceFile").html("<a style='color:black !important' href='" + msg.insuranceStatus.FilePath + "' target='_blank' >View Status File</a>");

                }
            //$("#InusranceStatus").html(msg.insuranceStatus.Profile.ProfileName);
            var profileName = msg.insuranceStatus.Profile.ProfileName;
            $("#InusranceStatus").html(profileName);

            switch (profileName) {
                case "Fully Approved":
                    $("#InusranceFile").css("background-color", "lightgreen");
                    $("#InusranceStatus").css("background-color", "lightgreen");
                    break;
                case "Partially Approved":
                    $("#InusranceFile").css("background-color", "#ffecb3");
                    $("#InusranceStatus").css("background-color", "#ffecb3");
                    break;
                case "Fully Rejected":
                    $("#InusranceFile").css("background-color", "lightcoral");
                    $("#InusranceStatus").css("background-color", "lightcoral");
                    break;
                case "Partially Approved with Inquiry":
                    $("#InusranceFile").css("background-color", "orange");
                    $("#InusranceStatus").css("background-color", "orange");
                    break;
                case "Fully Cancelled":
                    $("#InusranceFile").css("background-color", "teal");
                    $("#InusranceStatus").css("background-color", "teal");
                    break;
                case "Not Cover":
                    $("#InusranceFile").css("background-color", "lightgray");
                    $("#InusranceStatus").css("background-color", "lightgray");
                    break;
                default:
                    //$("#InusranceFile").css("background-color", "black");
                    //$("#InusranceStatus").css("background-color", "black");
                    //$("#InusranceStatus").css("color", "white"); // fallback to white if background is black
                    //$("#InusranceFile").css("color", "white"); // fallback to white if background is black
                    break;
            }
            }

        });
    }





    function GetInsuranceProcedureData(Id) {
     debugger
     var patientOrder = new Array();
        ////var departmentShortName = '@ViewBag.department';
     let docMovementShortName = '@ViewBag.DocMovementShortName';
     $("#loading-image").show();
     var _url = '@Url.Action("GetInsuranceProcedureData", "InsuranceInvoice")';
        var _data = "{id:'" + Id + "',shortName:'" + docMovementShortName + "'}";
     $.AjaxJsonAsynRequest(_url, _data, function (msg) {
         if (msg != null && msg != "[]" && msg != "") {
             debugger
              ////GetAllProcedurebyPatientCategory(175, null, '@ViewBag.department', '');
             patientOrder = $.parseJSON(msg);

             var e = jQuery.Event("keypress");
             e.keyCode = $.ui.keyCode.ENTER;

             var actualDate = patientOrder[0].DOB;
             debugger
             var d = new Date(patientOrder[0].DOB);
             var dt = ('0' + d.getDate()).slice(-2) + "/" + ('0' + (d.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "/" + d.getFullYear();
             $('#dpkDOB').val(ConvertToMonthDayYearFormatRe(new Date(patientOrder[0].DOB)));
             CalculateAge();
             $("#txtPatientVisitId").setValue(patientOrder[0].PatientVisitId);

             $("#txtProInvoiceId").setValue("");
             $("#txtProInsInvoiceId").setValue("");

             debugger
             $("#txtPatientAdmitId").setValue(patientOrder[0].PatientAdmitId);
             if (patientOrder[0].PartyName != '') {
                 $("#txtInsuranceCompanyName").setValue(patientOrder[0].PartyName);
                 $("#txtInsuranceCompanyId").setValue(patientOrder[0].InsuranceCompanyId);
             }
             if (patientOrder[0].PackageName != '') {
                 $("#txtPacakgeName").setValue(patientOrder[0].PackageName);
                 $("#txtInsurancePackageId").setValue(patientOrder[0].InsurancePackageId);
                 GetCopayDetailByPackageId(patientOrder[0].InsurancePackageId);
                 $("#txtPolicyNo").setValue(patientOrder[0].PolicyNo);
             }

             selectedProcCPTs = patientOrder;
             FillProOrderCPCTable(selectedProcCPTs);

             ProPaymentModeChangeEvent();

         }
     });
    }

    var FilterGenderCPT = new Array();

    function FilterCPTByGender(prefix) {

        if (prefix == "MALGEN") {
            FilterGenderCPT = new Array();
            for (var i = 0; i < cptArray.length; i++) {
                //if (cptArray[i].Section.length > 0)
                if (cptArray[i].IsGenderSpecificMale == "True") {
                    FilterGenderCPT.push(cptArray[i]);
                }
            }
        }
        else if (prefix == "FMLGEN") {
            FilterGenderCPT = new Array();
            for (var i = 0; i < cptArray.length; i++) {
                //if (cptArray[i].Section.length > 0)
                if (cptArray[i].IsGenderSpecificFemale == "True") {
                    FilterGenderCPT.push(cptArray[i]);
                }
            }
        }
        else {
            FilterGenderCPT = new Array();
            FilterGenderCPT = cptArray;
        }

    }
    function SetTitle(genID) {
        if (genID == '') {
            FilterGenderCPT = new Array();
            FilterGenderCPT = cptArray;
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < lstTitle.length; i++) {
            if (lstTitle[i].GenderProfileId == genID) {
                $("#ddl_Title").setValue(lstTitle[i].TitleId);

                for (var j = 0; j < lstGender.length; j++) {
                    if (lstGender[j].ProfileId == lstTitle[i].GenderProfileId) {
                        FilterCPTByGender(lstGender[j].ProfilePrefix);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }


    var patData = null;
    var empId = null;




    function DateDiff(dt1, dt2) {
        /*
         * setup 'empty' return object
         */
        var ret = { days: 0, months: 0, years: 0 };

        /*
         * If the dates are equal, return the 'empty' object
         */
        if (dt1 == dt2) return ret;

        /*
         * ensure dt2 > dt1
         */
        if (dt1 > dt2) {
            var dtmp = dt2;
            dt2 = dt1;
            dt1 = dtmp;
        }

        /*
         * First get the number of full years
         */

        var year1 = dt1.getFullYear();
        var year2 = dt2.getFullYear();

        var month1 = dt1.getMonth();
        var month2 = dt2.getMonth();

        var day1 = dt1.getDate();
        var day2 = dt2.getDate();

        /*
         * Set initial values bearing in mind the months or days may be negative
         */

        ret['years'] = year2 - year1;
        ret['months'] = month2 - month1;
        ret['days'] = day2 - day1;

        /*
         * Now we deal with the negatives
         */

        /*
         * First if the day difference is negative
         * eg dt2 = 13 oct, dt1 = 25 sept
         */
        if (ret['days'] < 0) {
            /*
             * Use temporary dates to get the number of days remaining in the month
             */
            var dtmp1 = new Date(dt1.getFullYear(), dt1.getMonth() + 1, 1, 0, 0, -1);

            var numDays = dtmp1.getDate();

            ret['months'] -= 1;
            ret['days'] += numDays;

        }

        /*
         * Now if the month difference is negative
         */
        if (ret['months'] < 0) {
            ret['months'] += 12;
            ret['years'] -= 1;
        }

        return ret;
    }


    function EnableDisableDOB(val) {
        try {
            if (val) {
                $('#dpkDOB').prop('disabled', true);
                $('#dpkDOB').setValue('');

                $("#txtYear").disable();
                $("#txtMonth").disable();
                $("#txtDay").disable();
                $("#txtHour").disable();
            }
            else {
                $('#dpkDOB').prop('disabled', false);

                $("#txtYear").enable();
                $("#txtMonth").enable();
                $("#txtDay").enable();
                $("#txtHour").enable();
            }
        }
        catch (e) {
            console.log(e.message);
        }
    }

    function OpenPrintPreview(rptLink) {
        if (isAdsServerFound) {
            $("#txtPath").setValue(rptLink);

            $("#objPrintPreview").attr("data", "http://" + window.location.host + rptLink + "#toolbar=0&scrollbar=0&navpanes=1");

            $("#objPrintPreview").load("http://" + window.location.host + rptLink + "#toolbar=0&scrollbar=0&navpanes=1");

            $("#modalboxPrintPreview").show("model");
        }
        else {
            //window.open("http://" + window.location.host + rptLink, '_blank');
            var _url = "http://" + window.location.host + rptLink;
            var win = window.open(_url, '_blank');
            if (win) {
                win.focus();
                win.print();
            }
            else
                alert('Please allow popups for this site');
        }
    }

    function CalculateCPCDiscount(ProTotalAmount, price, discount) {

        return cpcDisc;
    }

             $("#txtEmail").setValue((patientDetail.Email != null) ? patientDetail.Email : "");
             $("#ddl_Title").setValue((patientDetail.TitleId != null) ? patientDetail.TitleId : "");
             $("#ddl_SubTitle").setValue((patientDetail.SubTitleId != null) ? patientDetail.SubTitleId : "");
             $("#txtFatherName").setValue((patientDetail.FatherName != null) ? patientDetail.FatherName : "");

             Disabled();

             if (patientDetail.DOB == null) {
                 $("#chkDOB").setValue(true);
                 $("#chkDOB").disable();

                 $("#chkDOB").setValue(true);
                 EnableDisableDOB(true);
             }
             else {
                 $("#chkDOB").setValue(false);
                 debugger
                 var dob =ConvertToMonthDayYearFormatRe(new Date(parseInt(patientDetail.DOB.substr(6))));
                 //var d = new Date(patientOrder[0].DOB);

     });

    function ProCalculateRejectedPrice(rowNo, id, obj, price, e) {

        let insuranceGrossPrice = $("#txtProModeInsPrice" + id + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
        let CopayPer = $("#txtProCopayPercentage" + id + "_" + rowNo).getValue();

        let rejectedPrice = (insuranceGrossPrice - price).toFixed(2);
        $("#txtProRejectedColumn" + id + "_" + rowNo).setValue(rejectedPrice);
        ProCalculateCopayAmount(rowNo, id, obj, CopayPer);
        for (var j = 0; j < selectedProcCPTs.length; j++) {
            if (id == selectedProcCPTs[j].ServiceId) {

                selectedProcCPTs[j].RejectedPrice = parseFloat(rejectedPrice);
                break;

            }

        }

    }
    function ProCalculateDeductiblePrice(rowNo, id, obj, price, e) {
        $("#ProInsurance" + rowNo).prop("checked", true);
        ProHandlePaymentSelection(rowNo, id, obj, "insurance");
    }

    function ProCalculateCopayAmount(rowNo, id, obj, CopayPer, e) {

        let insuranceGrossPrice = $("#txtProApprovedColumn" + id + "_" + rowNo).getValue();

        let Copay = 0
        if (!isNaN(CopayPer) && CopayPer > 0) {
            Copay = (insuranceGrossPrice / 100) * CopayPer;
            Copay = Copay.toFixed(2);
        } else {
            Copay = 0; // fallback value or you can set to null or a default percentage
        }

        $("#txtProCopay" + id + "_" + rowNo).setValue(Copay);

        for (var j = 0; j < selectedProcCPTs.length; j++) {
            if (id == selectedProcCPTs[j].ServiceId) {

                selectedProcCPTs[j].Copay = parseFloat(Copay);
                break;

            }

        }
        $("#ProInsurance" + rowNo).prop("checked", true);
        ProHandlePaymentSelection(rowNo, id, obj, "insurance");
    }

    function ProChangePriceMode(id, price, e) {
        var priceMode = "NORPRC";
        ProTotalAmount = 0;
        ProChangePrice = "True";
        var found = false;
        for (var j = 0; j < selectedProcCPTs.length; j++) {
            if (id == selectedProcCPTs[j].ServiceId) {


                selectedProcCPTs[j].ServicePriceModePrefix = "NORPRC";
                selectedProcCPTs[j].Price = price;
                selectedProcCPTs[j].NORPRC = price;
                selectedProcCPTs[j].PriceForEdit = price;

                for (var k = 0; k < lstPriceMode.length; k++) {
                    if (lstPriceMode[k].ProfilePrefix == priceMode) {
                        selectedProcCPTs[j].ServicePriceModeId = lstPriceMode[k].ProfileId;
                    }
                }
            }
            if (selectedProcCPTs[j].Price != undefined) {
                ProTotalAmount = new Number(ProTotalAmount) + new Number(selectedProcCPTs[j].Price);
            }
        }
        ProTotalAmount = GetProTotalPrice();
        //ProTotalAmount = 0;
        if (ProTotalAmount != 0) {
            $("#txtProTotalAmount").setValue(ProTotalAmount);
            $("#txtProPayableAmount").setValue(ProTotalAmount);
            $("#txtProBalance").setValue(ProTotalAmount);
            // $("#txtProPaidAmount").setValue(ProTotalAmount); //saqib

            $("#txtTotalPro").empty();
            $("#txtTotalPro").append("Total Price = " + ProTotalAmount + "\tPKR");
            $("#txtTotalProTest").empty();
            $("#txtTotalProTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedProcCPTs.length + "");
            $("#txtProDiscountNet").trigger("onchange");


        }
        $("#txtTotalProTest").empty();
        $("#txtTotalProTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedProcCPTs.length + "");
    }

        }
    }
    var lstOldCptPrice = new Array();
    function ChangeDOB(val) {
        debugger
        if (!$("#dpkPatientOrderOn").validate(MSG_INFO)) return;
        if (!$("#txtYear").validate(MSG_INFO)) return;
        if (!$("#txtMonth").validate(MSG_INFO)) return;
        if (!$("#txtDay").validate(MSG_INFO)) return;
        if (!$("#txtHour").validate(MSG_INFO)) return;


        var year = $("#txtYear").getValue();
        var month = $("#txtMonth").getValue();
        var day = $("#txtDay").getValue();
        var hour = $("#txtHour").getValue();

        var actualDate = new Date($("#dpkPatientOrderOn").getValue());
        var newDate = new Date(actualDate.getFullYear() - new Number(year), actualDate.getMonth() - new Number(month), actualDate.getDate() - new Number(day));

        $("#dpkDOB").setValue(ConvertToMonthDayYearFormatRe(newDate));
    }
    function CalculateAge() {

        dateString = $("#dpkDOB").getValue();
        var parts = dateString.split('/');
        var day = parseInt(parts[0], 10);
        var month = parseInt(parts[1], 10) - 1; // Subtract 1 because months are zero-indexed in JavaScript
        var year = parseInt(parts[2], 10);
        var dob = new Date(year, month, day);
        if (!CheckIsValidDate(dob) || dob == null || dob == '') {
            return;
        }
        var now = new Date($("#dpkPatientOrderOn").getValue());
        var today = new Date(now.getYear(), now.getMonth(), now.getDate());

        var diff = dateDiff(now, dob); // HAMID

        var yearNow = now.getYear();
        var monthNow = now.getMonth();
        var dateNow = now.getDate();

        var yearDob = dob.getYear();
        var monthDob = dob.getMonth();
        var dateDob = dob.getDate();

        yearAge = yearNow - yearDob;

        if (monthNow >= monthDob)
            var monthAge = monthNow - monthDob;
        else {
            yearAge--;
            var monthAge = 12 + monthNow - monthDob;
        }

        if (dateNow >= dateDob)
            var dateAge = dateNow - dateDob;
        else {
            monthAge--;

            var dateAge = DaysInMonth(dob) + dateNow - dateDob;


            if (monthAge < 0) {
                monthAge = 11;
                yearAge--;
            }
        }
        var hours = 0;
        if (yearAge > 200) {
            ShowMessage('1', MSG_AGE);
            $("#txtAge").setValue('');
            $("#txtAge").focus();
            return;
        }
        dateAge = diff.days;
        //code by aamir for age box
        $("#txtYear").setValue(yearAge);
        $("#txtMonth").setValue(monthAge);
        $("#txtDay").setValue(dateAge);
        $("#txtHour").setValue("0");

        if ('@ViewBag.hour' != '') {
            $("#txtHour").setValue('@ViewBag.hour');
        }
    }
    function DaysInMonth(anyDateInMonth) {
        return new Date(anyDateInMonth.getYear(),
                        anyDateInMonth.getMonth() + 1,
                        0).getDate();
    }

    function dateDiff(dt1, dt2) {
        /*
         * setup 'empty' return object
         */
        var ret = { days: 0, months: 0, years: 0 };

        /*
         * If the dates are equal, return the 'empty' object
         */
        if (dt1 == dt2) return ret;

        /*
         * ensure dt2 > dt1
         */
        if (dt1 > dt2) {
            var dtmp = dt2;
            dt2 = dt1;
            dt1 = dtmp;
        }

        /*
         * First get the number of full years
         */

        var year1 = dt1.getFullYear();
        var year2 = dt2.getFullYear();

        var month1 = dt1.getMonth();
        var month2 = dt2.getMonth();

        var day1 = dt1.getDate();
        var day2 = dt2.getDate();

        /*
         * Set initial values bearing in mind the months or days may be negative
         */

        ret['years'] = year2 - year1;
        ret['months'] = month2 - month1;
        ret['days'] = day2 - day1;

        /*
         * Now we deal with the negatives
         */

        /*
         * First if the day difference is negative
         * eg dt2 = 13 oct, dt1 = 25 sept
         */
        if (ret['days'] < 0) {
            /*
             * Use temporary dates to get the number of days remaining in the month
             */
            var dtmp1 = new Date(dt1.getFullYear(), dt1.getMonth() + 1, 1, 0, 0, -1);

            var numDays = dtmp1.getDate();

            ret['months'] -= 1;
            ret['days'] += numDays;

        }

        /*
         * Now if the month difference is negative
         */
        if (ret['months'] < 0) {
            ret['months'] += 12;
            ret['years'] -= 1;
        }

        return ret;
    }


    function CheckIsValidDate(Date) {
        if (Object.prototype.toString.call(Date) === "[object Date]") {
            // it is a date
            if (isNaN(Date.getTime())) {  // d.valueOf() could also work
                return false;//Invalid Date
            }
            else {
                return true; //Correct Date
            }
        }
        else {
            return false; //InCorrect Date
        }
    }

    function CalculateProNetDiscount(val) {
        debugger
        ProChangePrice = "True";
        var price = GetProTotalPrice();
        $("#txtProTotalAmount").setValue(price);
        var balance = $("#txtProBalance").getValue();

        var disc = new Number(val);
        var paid = Math.floor(price - disc);


        if (price < disc) {
            ShowMessage('1', "You can maximum give discount Rs." + Math.floor(new Number(price)));
            $("#txtProDiscountNet").focus();
            validDiscount = false;
            return;
        }

        var perDisc = (disc / price) * 100;


        if (isNaN(perDisc)) {
            $("#txtProDiscountPer").setValue(0);
        }
        else {
            $("#txtProDiscountPer").setValue(new Number(perDisc).toFixed(2));
        }

        let CashReceived = $("#txtProCashReceived").getValue();

        if (CashReceived == "")
            CashReceived = 0;
        let CreditCardReceived = $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").getValue();
        if (CreditCardReceived == "")
            CreditCardReceived = 0;
        let PatientAccountReceived = $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
        if (PatientAccountReceived == "")
         PatientAccountReceived = 0;

        $("#txtProPayableAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - disc));
        $("#txtProPaidAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - disc));
        $("#txtProCurrentAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - disc));
       debugger
        value = $("#ddl_ProPaymode").getValue();
        if (value != "") {
            if (PaymentModeList.length > 0 && $.isArray(PaymentModeList) != null) {
                var PaymentModeObject = $.grep(PaymentModeList, function (item) {
                    return item.ProfileId.toString() === value;
                })[0];
                if (ProChangePrice == "True") {
                    if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PARPMD') {
                        $("#txtProCashReceived").setValue(price - disc);
                        $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                        $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#txtProCashReceived").setValue(0);
                        $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                        $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                    }
                    ProChangePrice = "False";
                }
                else {
                      if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PARPMD') {

                          $("#txtProCashReceived").setValue(Math.floor(price - CreditCardReceived - PatientAccountReceived - disAmount));
                          $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").setValue(CreditCardReceived);
                          $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").setValue(PatientAccountReceived);
                      }
                      else {
                                $("#txtProCashReceived").setValue(0);
                                $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                          $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                          }
                }
            }
        }

        $("#txtProTotalRecievedAmount").setValue($("#txtProPayableAmount").val());

        CalculateProRemainingAmount();


    }
    function GetProTotalPrice() {
        debugger
        var getTotalPrice = 0;
        //var getInsuraceTotalPrice=0
        try {
            if (ProCashArray != null) {
                for (var i = 0; i < ProCashArray.length; i++) {
                    var getPrice = $("#txtProModePrice" + ProCashArray[i].ServiceId + "_" + ProCashArray[i].IndexNo).getValue();

                    if (getPrice == "")
                        getPrice = 0;
                    getTotalPrice = new Number(getTotalPrice) + new Number(getPrice);
                }
            }
            return getTotalPrice;
        } catch (e) {
            console.log(e.message);
        }
    }
    function CalculateProPerDiscount(val) {
        var price = GetProTotalPrice();
        $("#txtProTotalAmount").setValue(price);


        var balance = $("#txtProBalance").getValue();


        var disc = new Number(val);
        var disAmount = Math.round((price / 100) * disc);
        var paid = Math.floor(price - disAmount);
        var dis = $("#txtProDiscountNet").getValue();
        if (disc > 100) {
            ShowMessage('1', "Invalid discount");
            $("#txtProDiscountPer").focus();
            validDiscount = false;
            return;
        }
        $("#txtProPayableAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - dis));
        $("#txtProPaidAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - dis));
        $("#txtProCashReceived").setValue(Math.floor(price - dis));
        $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
        $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
        $("#txtProTotalRecievedAmount").setValue($("#txtProReceived").val()); // saqib discount



        CalculateProRemainingAmount();

    }
    function CalculateProCurrentRemainingAmount() {
        var currentrecived = $("#txtProCurrentAmount").getValue();
        var payedAmount = $("#txtProPaidAmount").getValue();
        var payAbleAmount = $("#txtProPayableAmount").getValue();
        var netRecieved = $("#txtProReceived").getValue();

        var dueRecived = $("#txtProDueRecieved").getValue();


        var balanceAmount = new Number(netRecieved) + new Number(currentrecived) - new Number(dueRecived);
        balanceAmount = (new Number($("#txtProPayableAmount").getValue())) - (new Number($("#txtProReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProCurrentAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProReturn").getValue()));//new Number(payAbleAmount) - balanceAmount;

        if (balanceAmount < 0) {
            ShowMessage('1', MSG_BALANCE);
            $("#txtProCurrentAmount").setValue(0);
            $("#txtProPaidAmount").setValue(0);

            $("#txtProCurrentAmount").focus();
            $("#txtProBalance").setValue((new Number($("#txtProPayableAmount").getValue())) - (new Number($("#txtProReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProCurrentAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProReturn").getValue())));

            return false;
        }
        var totalRecievedAmount = new Number(netRecieved) + new Number(currentrecived);
        $("#txtProBalance").setValue(new Number($("#txtProPayableAmount").getValue()) - (new Number($("#txtProTotalRecievedAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProCurrentAmount").getValue())));

        $("#txtProPaidAmount").setValue(new Number($("#txtProReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProCurrentAmount").getValue()));
        $("#txtProTotalRecievedAmount").setValue(new Number($("#txtProReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProDueRecieved").getValue()));
        $("#txtProBalance").setValue((new Number($("#txtProPayableAmount").getValue())) - (new Number($("#txtProReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtProCurrentAmount").getValue())  + new Number($("#txtProReturn").getValue())));

        return true;
    }
    function CalculateProParitalReceivedAmount() {
        debugger
        $("#txtProCurrentAmount").setValue(0);
        var CashAmount = $("#txtProCashReceived").getValue();
        var CreditAmount = $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").getValue();
        var PatientAmount = $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
        var ProTotalAmount = new Number(CashAmount) + new Number(CreditAmount) + new Number(PatientAmount);
        $("#txtProCurrentAmount").setValue(ProTotalAmount);
        CalculateProCurrentRemainingAmount();
    }
    function CalculateProRemainingAmount() {
        debugger
        var payedAmount = $("#txtProPaidAmount").getValue();
        var payAbleAmount = $("#txtProPayableAmount").getValue();
        var netRecieved = $("#txtProReceived").getValue();
        var dueRecieved = $("#txtProDueRecieved").getValue();


        var currentRecived = new Number($("#txtProPayableAmount").getValue()) - new Number($("#txtProTotalRecievedAmount").getValue());


        debugger
        var balanceAmount = new Number($("#txtProPayableAmount").getValue())  - (new Number($("#txtProTotalRecievedAmount").getValue() ) );
        $("#txtProPaidAmount").setValue(new Number($("#txtProTotalRecievedAmount").getValue()) );
        if (balanceAmount < 0) {
            ShowMessage('1', MSG_BALANCE);
            $("#txtProCurrentAmount").setValue(0);
              $("#txtProPaidAmount").setValue(0);
            $("#txtProCurrentAmount").focus();
            return false;
        }

            $("#txtProBalance").setValue(balanceAmount);

        return true;
    }
    var filteredCPTArray;



    var scrollPosition;


    function LockScroll() {
        scrollPosition = [
                    self.pageXOffset || document.documentElement.scrollLeft || document.body.scrollLeft,
                    self.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop
        ];
        var html = jQuery('html'); // it would make more sense to apply this to body, but IE7 won't have that
        html.data('scroll-position', scrollPosition);
        html.data('previous-overflow', html.css('overflow'));
        html.css('overflow', 'hidden');
        window.scrollTo(scrollPosition[0], scrollPosition[1]);
    }

    function UnLockScroll() {
        // un-lock scroll position
        var html = jQuery('html');
        //var scrollPosition = html.data('scroll-position');
        html.data('scroll-position', scrollPosition);
        html.css('overflow', 'visible');
        window.scrollTo(scrollPosition[0], scrollPosition[1])
    }

    function filterByCPCCode(val, e) {
        $(document).unbind("keydown");
        filteredCPTArray = new Array();
        $("#tblProCPT").hide();
        $("#tblReferrals").hide();
        $("#tblReferralCodes").hide();
        $("#tblProCPCCode").hide();
        if (val.trim() === "") {
            $("#tblProCPCCode").hide();
            return;
        }
        //$("#tblReferrals").show();
        var dataw = filterProArray(val, FilterGenderCPT);
        //filteredCPTArray = GetCPTFilterObjectArray(dataw);
        $("#tblProCPCCode").show();
        var tbody = '';

        var tbody = '';
        tbody = GetCPTFilterTable(dataw);

        //if (e.keyCode == 13 && temp.length == 1) {
        //    searchByCode(temp[0].filterColumn);
        //}
        // SEARCHING PERFOME ON ENTER PRESS.
        if (e.keyCode == 13) {
            searchByCode(temp[0]);
        }

        //added by haroon 12/22/2014
        if (e.keyCode === 27) {
            $("#tblProCPCCode").hide();

        }
        //end
        if (tbody.trim() == '') {
            $("#tblProCPCCode").hide();
            $(document).unbind("keydown");
        }
        else {
            BindfilterProArrayArrowKeys("tblProCPCCode", "txtLabCPTCode", "searchByCode");
        }

        $("#tblProCPCCode").html(tbody);
    }

    function searchByCode(obj) {
        $("#MSG").hide();
        $("#loading").show();
        //var code = $("#" + id).getValue();
        var isFound = false;
        for (var i = 0; i < FilterGenderCPT.length; i++) {
            if (FilterGenderCPT[i].LabTest.TestCode != null)
                if (FilterGenderCPT[i].LabTest.TestCode.toUpperCase() == obj.LabTest.TestCode.toUpperCase()) {
                    isFound = true;
                    AddCPT(FilterGenderCPT[i], false);
                }
        }
        if (!isFound) {
            showError(true, "No match found!");
        }
        $("#txtProCPTCode").setValue('');
        $("#txtProCPTCode").focus();
        $("#tblProCPCCode").hide();
    }

    function Clear() {
        labOrderId = 0;
        isCheckZero = true;
        var d = new Date();
        var dt = ('0' + (d.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "/" + ('0' + d.getDate()).slice(-2) + "/" + d.getFullYear();
        $('#dpkPatientOrderOn').val(dt);
        $("#txtProPatientOrderSetId").setValue("");
        $("#txtPatientId").setValue("");
        $("#txtInsurancePartyLocationId").setValue("");
        $("#txtProInvoiceId").setValue("");
        $("#txtLabInvoiceId").setValue("");
        $("#txtLabInsInvoiceId").setValue("");
        $("#txtRadInvoiceId").setValue("");
        $("#txtRadInsInvoiceId").setValue("");
        //patientInquiryId = 0;
        $("input[type='text']").each(function () {
            if (this.id != "dpkPatientOrderOn" && this.id != "txtDepartmentId") {
                $(this).clear();
            }
        });
        $("select").each(function () {
            if (this.id != "ddl_PatientCategory" && this.id != "ddl_PatientType" && this.id != "ddl_ProPaymode" && this.id != "ddl_LabPartyLocationId") {
                $(this).clear();
                $(this).val("");
            }
        });
        $("#InvoiceCategory").val(0);
        $("#InvoiceCategory").attr("disabled", false);

        selectedProcCPTs = new Array();
        $("#divCompany").hide();
        $("#divPatCompany").hide();
        $("#divPatEmployee").hide();
        ProTotalAmount = 0;
        $('#tblProOrderCPC tbody').empty();

        $("#txtYear").setValue(0);
        $("#txtMonth").setValue(0);
        $("#txtDay").setValue(0);
        $("#txtHour").setValue(0);

        $("#txtTotalPro").html('');
        $("#txtTotalPro").append("Total Price = " + 0 + "\tPKR");
        $("#txtTotalProTest").empty();
        $("#txtTotalProTest").append("Total Test = " + 0 + "");

        $("#txtProDiscountNet").setValue(0);
        $("#txtProDiscountPer").setValue(0);
        $("#txtProReceived").setValue(0);
        $("#txtProDueRecieved").setValue(0);
        $("#txtProReturn").setValue(0);
        Enable();

        var isDOBAvailable = $("#chkDOB").getValue();
        EnableDisableDOB(isDOBAvailable);

        //$("#ddl_Title").setValue("1");

        @*if ($("#ddl_PatientCategory").getValue() != 175)
            GetAllCPCbyPatientCategory(175, null, '@ViewBag.department');*@
        $("#ddl_PatientCategory").setValue(175);
        $("#InvoiceCategory").val(0);


        $("#txtMobile").focus();
        $("#txtPatientName").attr("disabled", false);
        $("#txtMobile").attr("disabled", false);

        var IsROBillCategOnReceptionLab = '@ViewBag.IsROBillCategOnReceptionLab';

        if (IsROBillCategOnReceptionLab == "True") {
            $("#ddl_PatientCategory").attr("disabled", true);
        }
        else
            $("#ddl_PatientCategory").attr("disabled", false);



        $("#ddl_Title").prop("disabled", false);
        $("#ddl_Gender").prop("disabled", false);
        $("#txtCNIC").prop("disabled", false);
        $("#txtEmail").prop("disabled", false);
        $("#txtYear").prop("disabled", false);
        $("#txtMonth").prop("disabled", false);
        $("#txtDay").prop("disabled", false);
        $("#txtHour").prop("disabled", false);
        $("#dpkDOB").prop("disabled", false);
        ChangeDOB($("#txtYear").getValue());

    }

    }

    function chkFutureDate(val) {
        var cDate = new Date();
        var date = (cDate.getMonth() + 1) + "/" + cDate.getDate() + "/" + cDate.getFullYear();
        if (new Date(val) > new Date(date)) {
            ShowMessage('1', "DOB cannot greater then current date");
            $("#dpkDOB").setFocus();
            // Corrected by Murtaza. 25 NOV 2014
            return false;
        }
        else
            return true;
        // end correction
    }

    function ProPaymentModeChangeEvent() {
        debugger
        value = $("#ddl_ProPaymode").getValue();
        if (value != "") {
            if (PaymentModeList.length > 0 && $.isArray(PaymentModeList) != null) {
                var PaymentModeObject = $.grep(PaymentModeList, function (item) {
                    return item.ProfileId.toString() === value;
                })[0];
                if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PATPMD') {
                    $("#divProPatientAdvance").show();
                }
                else {
                    $("#divProPatientAdvance").hide();
                }
                if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PARPMD') {
                    $("#divProCashReceived").show();
                    $("#divProCreditCardReceived").show();
                    $("#divProPatientAccountReceived").show();
                    $("#divProPatientAdvance").show();
                    $("#txtProCurrentAmount").disable();
                    let ReceivedAmmount = $("#txtProCurrentAmount").getValue();

                    let CashReceived = $("#txtProCashReceived").getValue();

                    if (CashReceived == "")
                        CashReceived = 0;
                    let CreditCardReceived = $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").getValue();
                    if (CreditCardReceived == "")
                        CreditCardReceived = 0;
                    let PatientAccountReceived = $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
                    if (PatientAccountReceived == "")
                        PatientAccountReceived = 0;
                    $("#txtProCashReceived").setValue(ReceivedAmmount - CreditCardReceived - PatientAccountReceived);
                    $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").setValue(CreditCardReceived);
                    $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").setValue(PatientAccountReceived);


                }
                else {
                    $("#divProCashReceived").hide();
                    $("#divProCreditCardReceived").hide();
                    $("#divProPatientAccountReceived").hide();
                    $("#txtProCashReceived").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtProCurrentAmount").enable();
                    if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PATPMD') {
                        $("#divProPatientAdvance").show();
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#divProPatientAdvance").hide();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function ProHandlePaymentSelection(rowNo, serviceId,seviceObj, type) {


        var ProInsuranceCheckbox = document.getElementById("ProInsurance" + rowNo);
        var ProCashCheckbox = document.getElementById("ProCash" + rowNo);

        if (type === "insurance") {
            if (ProInsuranceCheckbox.checked) {
                ProCashCheckbox.checked = false; // Uncheck Cash if Insurance is checked
                ProRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
                var ProObjIns = new Object();
                ProObjIns.IndexNo = rowNo;
                ProObjIns.ServiceId = serviceId;
                ProObjIns.Quantity = $("#txtProQuantity" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjIns.Instruction = $("#txtProInstruction" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjIns.NORPRC = $("#txtProModeInsPrice" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjIns.CopayPer = $("#txtProCopayPercentage" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjIns.Copay = $("#txtProCopay" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjIns.CopayPercentage = $("#txtProCopayPercentage" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjIns.InsuranceDiscPer = $("#txtProInsuranceDiscountPer" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjIns.InsuranceDiscAmount = $("#txtProInsuranceDiscountPrice" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();

                ProObjIns.Deductible = $("#txtProDeductible" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjIns.ApprovedPrice = $("#txtProApprovedColumn" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjIns.RejectedPrice = $("#txtProRejectedColumn" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjIns.IsInsuranceClaim = true;
                ProObjIns.PatientPrescribeServiceId = seviceObj.PatientPrescribeServiceId;
                ProObjIns.PatientPrescribeTreatmentPlanDetailId = seviceObj.PatientPrescribeTreatmentPlanDetailId;

                ProInsuranceArray.push(ProObjIns); // Add to Insurance array
            } else {
                ProRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
            }
        } else if (type === "cash") {
            if (ProCashCheckbox.checked) {
                ProInsuranceCheckbox.checked = false; // Uncheck Insurance if Cash is checked
                ProRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
                var ProObjCash = new Object();
                ProObjCash.IndexNo = rowNo;
                ProObjCash.ServiceId = serviceId;
                ProObjCash.Quantity = $("#txtProQuantity" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjCash.Instruction = $("#txtProInstruction" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjCash.NORPRC = $("#txtProModePrice" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                ProObjCash.IsInsuranceClaim = false;
                ProObjCash.PatientPrescribeServiceId = seviceObj.PatientPrescribeServiceId;
                ProObjCash.PatientPrescribeTreatmentPlanDetailId = seviceObj.PatientPrescribeTreatmentPlanDetailId;
                ProCashArray.push(ProObjCash); // Add to Cash array
            } else {
                ProRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
            }
        }
        ProUpdateInvoiceAmounts();
        CalculateGrandTotal();
    }

    function ProRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo) {
        ProCashArray = ProCashArray.filter(item => !(item.ServiceId == serviceId && item.IndexNo == rowNo));
        ProInsuranceArray = ProInsuranceArray.filter(item => !(item.ServiceId == serviceId && item.IndexNo == rowNo));
    }

    //function ProRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo) {

    function CalculateGrandTotal() {

        $("#htmlGrandTotal").html('');
        let tempTotal = $("#txtProTotalAmount").getValue();
        let tempTotalCopay = $("#InsuranceProTotalCopay").getValue();
        if (tempTotal == null || tempTotal == "") {
            tempTotal=0
        }
        if (tempTotalCopay == null || tempTotalCopay == "") {
            tempTotalCopay = 0
        }
        let tempGrandTotal = (tempTotal * 1) + (tempTotalCopay * 1);
        $("#htmlGrandTotal").html('Grand Total: ' + tempGrandTotal + ' QAR');
    }

    function ProUpdateInvoiceAmounts() {
        var cashTotal = ProCashArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.NORPRC * item.Quantity), 0);
        var insuranceTotal = ProInsuranceArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.NORPRC * item.Quantity), 0);

        var totalCopay = ProInsuranceArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + ((item.Copay * 1) + (item.Deductible * 1) + (item.RejectedPrice * 1)), 0);
        var totalTotalInsuranceDiscAmount = ProInsuranceArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + ((item.InsuranceDiscAmount * 1)), 0);
        $("#txtProTotalAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
        $("#txtProPayableAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
        $("#txtProCurrentAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
        $("#txtProPaidAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
        $("#txtProBalance").setValue(0);
        $("#txtProTotalRecievedAmount").setValue(cashTotal);

        $("#InsuranceProtxtTotalAmount").setValue(insuranceTotal);

        $("#InsuranceProTotalCopay").setValue(totalCopay.toFixed(2));
        $("#InsuranceProtxtInsuranceDiscountAmount").setValue(totalTotalInsuranceDiscAmount.toFixed(2));
        $("#InsuranceProtxtPayableByInsurance").setValue(insuranceTotal - totalTotalInsuranceDiscAmount - totalCopay);
        if (cashTotal == 0) {
            $("#txtProDiscountNet").setValue(cashTotal);
        }
        $("#txtProDiscountNet").trigger("change");


    }

    function GetPatientObjData() {
        debugger

        try {
            var isDOBAvailable = $("#chkDOB").getValue();
            var patientId = $("#txtPatientId").getValue();
            var counter = 0;
            //Usman Added
            if (!$("#txtMobile").validate(MSG_REQ)) counter++;
            //if ($("#txtDepartmentComponentId").getValue() == "") {
            //    $("#txtDepartmentComponentId").select2('open');
            //    return;

            //}
            if (!isDOBAvailable)
                if (!$("#dpkDOB").validate(MSG_REQ)) counter++;
            if (!$("#ddl_Gender").validate(MSG_REQ)) counter++;
            if (!$("#txtPatientName").validate(MSG_REQ)) counter++;
            if (!$("#ddl_PatientCategory").validate(MSG_REQ)) counter++;
            var dob = $("#dpkDOB").getValue();
            var year = $("#txtYear").getValue();
            var month = $("#txtMonth").getValue();
            var day = $("#txtDay").getValue();
            var hour = $("#txtHour").getValue();
            if (counter > 0) return;

            if ($("#ddl_PatientCategory").getValue() == "86") {
                if ($("#ddl_EmployeePatient").getValue().trim() == "") {
                    ShowMessage(1, "Please select employee");
                    return;
                }
            }
            if ($("#ddl_PatientCategory").getValue() == "72") {
                if ($("#ddl_Company").getValue().trim() == "" || $("#ddl_CompanyPatient").getValue().trim() == "") {
                    ShowMessage(1, "Please select company patient");
                    return;
                }
            }

            if (isFloor && $("#txtBlockFloorId").getValue().trim() == "") {            ///Added by Hassaan
                ShowMessage('1', "Please select Floor.");
                return;
            }


            var patientCat = $("#ddl_PatientCategory").getValue();
            var patientType = $("#ddl_PatientType").getValue();
            var title = $("#ddl_Title").getValue();
            var subtitle = $("#ddl_SubTitle").getValue();
            var patientFatherName = $("#txtFatherName").getValue();
            var patientName = $("#txtPatientName").getValue();
            var patientMiddleName = $("#txtPatientMiddleName").getValue();
            var patientLastName = $("#txtPatientLastName").getValue();
            var gender = $("#ddl_Gender").getValue();
            var bloodGroup = $("#ddl_BloodGroup").getValue();
            if (!isDOBAvailable) {
                if (year == "0" && month == "0" && day == "0" && hour == "0") {
                    ShowMessage('1', "Please enter age");
                    $("#txtYear").focus();
                    return;
                }
            }
            var mobile = $("#txtMobile").getValue();
            var cinic = $("#txtCNIC").getValue();
            var email = $("#txtEmail").getValue();


            var comp = $("#ddl_Company").getValue();
            var empID = $("#txtEmployeeID").getValue();

            var isfinanreq = $("#chkIsFinancialAssistanceRequired").getValue();
            var needLogin = $("#chkNeedLogin").getValue();
            var objPat = new Object();
            objPat.Address = new Object();

            if (patientId == '') {
                patientId = 0;
            }
            if (mobile == "____-_______")
                mobile = "";

            objPat.PatientId = patientId;

            for (var i = 0, max = lstPatientCategory.length; i < max; i++) {
                if (lstPatientCategory[i].ProfileId == patientCat) {
                    var profilePrefix = lstPatientCategory[i].ProfilePrefix;
                    if (profilePrefix == CORTYPE) {
                        objPat.PartyLocationId = $("#txtPartyLocationId9").val();
                    }
                    else
                        objPat.PartyLocationId = null;

                }
            }
            objPat.PatientTypeProfileId = patientType;
            objPat.TitleId = title;
            objPat.SubTitleId = subtitle;
            objPat.FirstName = patientFirstName;

            if (patientMiddleName == null || patientMiddleName == "null") {
                patientMiddleName = "";
            }
            if (patientLastName == null || patientLastName == "null") {
                patientLastName = "";
            }
            objPat.MiddleName = patientMiddleName;
            objPat.LastName = patientLastName;
            objPat.PatientName = patientFirstName + " " + patientMiddleName.trim() + " " + patientLastName.trim();
            objPat.FatherName = patientFatherName;
            objPat.GenderProfileId = gender;
            objPat.BloodProfileId = bloodGroup;
            if (!isDOBAvailable) {
                objPat.DOB = new Date(dob);
            }
            objPat.CNIC = cinic;
            objPat.Email = email
            objPat.Mobile1 = mobile
            objPat.PartyId = comp;
            objPat.NeedLogin = needLogin;
            objPat.InsurancePartyLocationId = $("#txtInsurancePartyLocationId").getValue();

            objPat.IsFinancialAssistanceRequired = isfinanreq;

            if ($("#txtEmplyeeId1").getValue() != 0) {
                objPat.EmployeeId = $("#txtEmplyeeId1").getValue();
            }


            return objPat;
        } catch (e) {
            console.log(e.message);
        }
    }


    function GetProInvoiceObjCash() {

        try {
            var objVoucher = new Object();
            objVoucher.PayModeProfileId = $("#ddl_InsuranceProPaymode").getValue();
            var objInvoice = new Object();

            objInvoice.InvoiceId = $("#txtProInvoiceId").getValue();
            objInvoice.VoucherId = $("#txtProVoucherId").getValue();
            objInvoice.ReceiptVoucherId = $("#txtProReceiptVoucherId").getValue();
            objInvoice.CashReceived = $("#txtProCashReceived").getValue();
            objInvoice.CreditCardReceived = $("#txtProCreditCardReceived").getValue();
            objInvoice.PatientAccountReceived = $("#txtProPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
            objInvoice.TotalReceived = $("#txtProPaidAmount").getValue();

            objVoucher.VoucherId = $("#txtProVoucherReceiptId").getValue();
            objVoucher.TotalCredit = objInvoice.TotalReceived;
            objVoucher.TotalDebit = objInvoice.TotalReceived;

            objInvoice.Voucher1 = objVoucher;

            return objInvoice;
        } catch (e) {

        }

    }

    function GetProCashOrderDetailObj() {
        var ProTotalAmount = $("#txtProTotalAmount").getValue();
        var discountNet = $("#txtProDiscountNet").getValue();
        var discPer = $("#txtProDiscountPer").getValue();
        var payAmount = $("#txtProPayableAmount").getValue();


        var paidAmount = $("#txtProPaidAmount").getValue();
        var balance = $("#txtProBalance").getValue();
        var miscAmount = 0;
        var tax = 0;

        let profilePrefix = "";

        var ServicePackageId = 0;
        var lstCashOrderDetail = new Array();

        var lineID = 1;

        for (var i = 0; i < ProCashArray.length; i++) {
            debugger
            var cpcDiscount = 0;
            var grossAmount = 0;
            var amount = 0;

            var objCashOrdDetail = new Object();
            if (ProCashArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId != null) {
                objCashOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = ProCashArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
            }
            objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailSet = new Object();
            if (ProCashArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId != undefined) {
                objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = ProCashArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId;

            }
            else {
                objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = 0;
            }

            if (profilePrefix != "GRTPAT") {
                if (ProCashArray[i].ServicePackageId == undefined) {
                    if (objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                        if (ProCashArray[i].PriceForEdit == 0) {
                            ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (ProCashArray[i].NORPRC != undefined)
                            if (ProCashArray[i].NORPRC == 0) {
                                ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                                return;
                            }
                    }
                }
            }

            objCashOrdDetail.DiscPercent = discPer;

            if (ProCashArray[i].ServicePackageId != undefined) {
                ServicePackageId = ProCashArray[i].ServicePackageId;
                objCashOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = ProCashArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
            }
            objCashOrdDetail.PriceModeProfileId = ProCashArray[i].ServicePriceModeId;

            objCashOrdDetail.ServiceId = ProCashArray[i].ServiceId
            objCashOrdDetail.PatientPrescribeServiceId = ProCashArray[i].PatientPrescribeServiceId;
            objCashOrdDetail.PatientPrescribeTreatmentPlanDetailId = ProCashArray[i].PatientPrescribeTreatmentPlanDetailId;

            if (ProCashArray[i].IsSTAT) {
                cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(ProTotalAmount, ProCashArray[i].STATPrice, discountNet);
                grossAmount = new Number(ProCashArray[i].STATPrice) - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                amount = ProCashArray[i].STATPrice;
            }
            else {
                if (objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                    cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(ProTotalAmount, ProCashArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                    grossAmount = new Number(ProCashArray[i].NORPRC) - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                    amount = ProCashArray[i].NORPRC;
                }
                else {
                    cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(ProTotalAmount, ProCashArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                    grossAmount = new Number(ProCashArray[i].NORPRC) - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                    amount = ProCashArray[i].NORPRC;
                }


            }
            objCashOrdDetail.IsInsuranceClaim = ProCashArray[i].IsInsuranceClaim;
            objCashOrdDetail.Amount = amount;
            objCashOrdDetail.Price = amount;
            objCashOrdDetail.Quantity = ProCashArray[i].Quantity || 1;
            //objCashOrdDetail.Quantity = Quantity;
            objCashOrdDetail.DiscPerUnit = cpcDiscount;
            objCashOrdDetail.DiscountAmount = cpcDiscount;
            objCashOrdDetail.GrossAmount = grossAmount;

            objCashOrdDetail.MiscPerUnit = 0;
            objCashOrdDetail.MiscAmount = 0;
            objCashOrdDetail.NetAmount = grossAmount;
            objCashOrdDetail.NetPrice = grossAmount;
            objCashOrdDetail.ReceivableAmount = grossAmount;
            objCashOrdDetail.TaxAmount = 0;
            objCashOrdDetail.TaxPercent = 0;
            objCashOrdDetail.LineDescription = ProCashArray[i].Remarks;

            objCashOrdDetail.ReportDateTime = ProCashArray[i].ReportDateTime;
            objCashOrdDetail.IsSampleBrought = ProCashArray[i].IsSampleBrought;
            lstCashOrderDetail.push(objCashOrdDetail);
            lineID++;
        }

        return lstCashOrderDetail;
    }

    function GetProINSOrderDetailObj() {

        let profilePrefix = "";

        var ServicePackageId = 0;
        let discountNet = 0;
        let ProTotalAmount = $("#InsuranceProtxtTotalAmount").getValue();
        var lstInsOrderDetail = new Array();
        let lineID = 1;
        for (var i = 0; i < ProInsuranceArray.length; i++) {
            debugger
            var cpcDiscount = 0;
            var grossAmount = 0;
            var amount = 0;
            var objINSOrdDetail = new Object();
            if (ProInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId != null) {
                objINSOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = ProInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
            }
            objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailSet = new Object();
            if (ProInsuranceArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId != undefined) {
                objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = ProInsuranceArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId;
            }
            else {
                objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = 0;
            }
            if (profilePrefix != "GRTPAT") {
                if (ProInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageId == undefined) {
                    if (objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                        if (ProInsuranceArray[i].PriceForEdit == 0) {
                            ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (ProInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC != undefined)
                            if (ProInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC == 0) {
                                ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                                return;
                            }
                    }
                }
            }

            objINSOrdDetail.DiscPercent = 0;
            if (ProInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageId != undefined) {
                ServicePackageId = ProInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageId;
                objINSOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = ProInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
            }
            objINSOrdDetail.PriceModeProfileId = ProInsuranceArray[i].ServicePriceModeId;

            objINSOrdDetail.ServiceId = ProInsuranceArray[i].ServiceId
            objINSOrdDetail.PatientPrescribeServiceId = ProInsuranceArray[i].PatientPrescribeServiceId;
            objINSOrdDetail.PatientPrescribeTreatmentPlanDetailId = ProInsuranceArray[i].PatientPrescribeTreatmentPlanDetailId;

            if (ProInsuranceArray[i].IsSTAT) {
                cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(ProTotalAmount, ProInsuranceArray[i].STATPrice, discountNet);
                grossAmount = new Number(ProInsuranceArray[i].STATPrice); //- new Number(cpcDiscount);
                amount = ProCashArray[i].STATPrice;
            }
            else {
                if (objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                    cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(ProTotalAmount, ProInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                    grossAmount = new Number(ProInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC);// - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                    amount = ProInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC;
                }
                else {
                    cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(ProTotalAmount, ProInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                    grossAmount = new Number(ProInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC);// - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                    amount = ProInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC;
                }
            }

            objINSOrdDetail.IsInsuranceClaim = ProInsuranceArray[i].IsInsuranceClaim;
            objINSOrdDetail.Amount = amount;
            objINSOrdDetail.Price = (ProInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (ProInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (ProInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
            objINSOrdDetail.CopayPer = ProInsuranceArray[i].CopayPer;
            objINSOrdDetail.Copay = ProInsuranceArray[i].Copay;
            objINSOrdDetail.Deductible = ProInsuranceArray[i].Deductible;
            objINSOrdDetail.ApprovedPrice = ProInsuranceArray[i].ApprovedPrice;
            objINSOrdDetail.RejectedPrice = ProInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice;
            objINSOrdDetail.InsuranceDiscPer = ProInsuranceArray[i].InsuranceDiscPer;
            objINSOrdDetail.InsuranceDiscAmount = ProInsuranceArray[i].InsuranceDiscAmount;
            objINSOrdDetail.Quantity = ProInsuranceArray[i].Quantity || 1;
            objINSOrdDetail.DiscPerUnit = cpcDiscount;
            objINSOrdDetail.DiscountAmount = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.GrossAmount = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.MiscPerUnit = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.MiscAmount = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.NetAmount = (ProInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (ProInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (ProInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
            objINSOrdDetail.NetPrice = (ProInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (ProInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (ProInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
            objINSOrdDetail.ReceivableAmount = (ProInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (ProInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (ProInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
            objINSOrdDetail.TaxAmount = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.TaxPercent = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.LineDescription = ProInsuranceArray[i].Remarks;
            objINSOrdDetail.ReportDateTime = ProInsuranceArray[i].ReportDateTime;
            objINSOrdDetail.IsSampleBrought = ProInsuranceArray[i].IsSampleBrought;
            lstInsOrderDetail.push(objINSOrdDetail);
            lineID++;
        }

        return lstInsOrderDetail;
    }

    function GetPatientOrderObjData() {
        debugger
        let patientId = $("#txtPatientId").getValue();

        var remarks = $("#txtRemarks").getValue();
        let ServicePackageId = 0;

        var obj = new Object();
        for (var i = 0, max = lstPatientCategory.length; i < max; i++) {
            if (lstPatientCategory[i].ProfileId == patientCat) {
                var profilePrefix = lstPatientCategory[i].ProfilePrefix;
                if (profilePrefix == CORTYPE) {
                    obj.InvoicePartyLocationId = $("#txtPartyLocationId9").getValue();
                }
            }
        }
        InsuranceCompanyName = $("#txtInsuranceCompanyName").getValue();

        if (InsuranceCompanyName != "") {
            obj.InvoicePartyLocationId = $("#txtInsuranceCompanyId").getValue();
        }

        InsurancePackageName = $("#txtPacakgeName").getValue();

        if (InsurancePackageName != "") {
            obj.InsurancePackageId = $("#txtInsurancePackageId").getValue();
        }
        obj.Remarks = remarks;

        obj.DepartmentId = $("#txtDepartmentId").val();
        obj.PatientOrderSet = new Object();
        obj.Invoice = new Object();
        obj.PatientInquiry = new Object();
        obj.ParentPatientInquiryId = $("#txtParentPatientInquiryId").getValue();
        obj.PatientInquiry.BlockFloorId = $("#txtBlockFloorId").getValue();          //added by Hassaan
        obj.PatientInquiry.ScheduleTypeProfileId = $("#txtScheduleTypeProfileId").getValue();          //added by Hassaan

        obj.PatientOrderSet.BillCategoryProfileId = $("#ddl_PatientCategory").getValue();

        obj.PatientOrderSet.PatientAdmitId = $("#txtPatientAdmitId").getValue();
        obj.PatientOrderSet.PatientRequisitionId = $("#txtPatientRequisitionId").getValue();
        if (ServicePackageId != 0)
            obj.PatientOrderSet.ServicePackageId = ServicePackageId;

        obj.ParentPatientOrderId = $("#txtParentPatientOrderId").getValue();
        let isDOBAvailables = $("#chkDOB").getValue();
        let dobo = $("#dpkDOB").getValue();
        let yearo = $("#txtYear").getValue();
        let montho = $("#txtMonth").getValue();
        let dayo = $("#txtDay").getValue();
        let houro = $("#txtHour").getValue();
        let ageo = yearo + " Y " + montho + " M " + dayo + " D " + houro + " H ";

        if (!isDOBAvailables) {
            obj.PatientAge = ageo;
            obj.PatientAgeYear = yearo;
            obj.PatientAgeMonth = montho;
            obj.PatientAgeDay = dayo;
            obj.PatientAgeHour = houro;
        }
        //obj.ShiftId = shift;
        //$("#dpkPatientOrderOn").setValue(patientOrder[0].PatientOrderOn);
        obj.PatientOrderOn = $("#dpkPatientOrderOn").getValue();


        obj.PatientVisitId = $("#txtPatientVisitId").getValue();

        //Usman Added
        debugger
        var labLabPartyLocationId = $("#ddl_LabPartyLocationId").getValue();
        obj.LabPartyLocationId = labLabPartyLocationId;

        obj.PatientId = patientId;

        if ($("#txtEmplyeeId").getValue() != 0) {
            obj.RefEmployeeId = $("#txtEmplyeeId").getValue();
        }
        if ($("#txtEmplyeeId1").getValue() != 0) {
            obj.InvoiceEmployeeId = $("#txtEmplyeeId1").getValue();
            obj.IsInternalRef = true;
        }

        if ($("#InvoiceCategory").getValue() == "1")
            obj.IsCreditInvoice = true;
        else
            obj.IsCreditInvoice = false;
        return obj;
    }

    function GetProPatientOrderObjForCash() {
        debugger
        var ProTotalAmount = $("#txtProTotalAmount").getValue();
        var discountNet = $("#txtProDiscountNet").getValue();
        var discPer = $("#txtProDiscountPer").getValue();
        var payAmount = $("#txtProPayableAmount").getValue();


        var paidAmount = $("#txtProPaidAmount").getValue();
        var balance = $("#txtProBalance").getValue();
        var miscAmount = 0;
        var tax = 0;
        var cashObj = new Object();
        cashObj = GetPatientOrderObjData();
        cashObj.DocMovement = new Object();
        cashObj.DocMovement.ShortName = 'PROPOD';
        cashObj.PatientOrderSet.DepartmentComponentId = $("#txtDepartmentComponentId").getValue();
        cashObj.PatientOrderSet.PaymentMethodProfileId = $("#ddl_ProPaymode").getValue();
        cashObj.PatientOrderSet.PatientOrderSetId = $("#txtProPatientOrderSetId").getValue();
        cashObj.PatientOrderId = $("#txtProPatientOrderId").getValue();

        cashObj.InvoiceId = $("#txtProInvoiceId").getValue();
        cashObj.PatientOrderSet.IsInsuranceOrder = false;
        cashObj.TotalAmount = Math.floor(ProTotalAmount);
        cashObj.TotalAmountDecimal = ProTotalAmount;
        cashObj.TotalDiscount = discountNet;
        cashObj.TotalGross = payAmount;
        cashObj.TotalMisc = miscAmount;
        cashObj.TotalNet = payAmount;
        cashObj.TotalReceivable = payAmount;
        cashObj.TotalTax = tax;
        cashObj.DiscPercent = discPer;
        cashObj.Patient = new Object();
        cashObj.Patient = GetPatientObjData();
        cashObj.PatientOrderDetails = new Array();
        cashObj.PatientOrderDetails = GetProCashOrderDetailObj();
        cashObj.Invoice = new Object();
        cashObj.Invoice = GetProInvoiceObjCash();

        return cashObj;
    }
    function GetProPatientOrderObjForInsurance() {

        debugger



        var insurancetotalAmount = $("#InsuranceProtxtTotalAmount").getValue();
        let totalCopay = $("#InsuranceProTotalCopay").getValue();
        var PayablebyInsurance = $("#InsuranceProtxtPayableByInsurance").getValue();
        var insuranceDiscountAmount = $("#InsuranceProtxtInsuranceDiscountAmount").getValue();

        var INSObj = new Object();
        INSObj = GetPatientOrderObjData();
        INSObj.DocMovement = new Object();
        INSObj.DocMovement.ShortName = 'PROPOD';
        INSObj.PatientOrderSet.DepartmentComponentId = $("#txtDepartmentComponentId").getValue();
        INSObj.PatientOrderSet.PaymentMethodProfileId = $("#ddl_InsuranceProPaymode").getValue();
        INSObj.PatientOrderSet.PatientOrderSetId = $("#txtProInsPatientOrderSetId").getValue();
        INSObj.PatientOrderId = $("#txtProInsPatientOrderId").getValue();
        INSObj.PatientOrderSet.IsInsuranceOrder = true;
        INSObj.TotalAmount = Math.floor(insurancetotalAmount);;
        INSObj.TotalAmountDecimal = insurancetotalAmount;
        INSObj.TotalCopay = totalCopay;
        INSObj.TotalDiscount = 0;
        INSObj.TotalGross = (totalCopay * 1);
        INSObj.TotalMisc = 0;
        INSObj.TotalNet = 0;
        INSObj.TotalReceivable = (totalCopay * 1)

        INSObj.PayableToInsurance = PayablebyInsurance;
        INSObj.InsuranceDiscountAmount = insuranceDiscountAmount;
        INSObj.TotalTax = 0;

        INSObj.Patient = new Object();
        INSObj.Patient = GetPatientObjData();

        INSObj.PatientOrderDetails = new Array();
        INSObj.PatientOrderDetails = GetProINSOrderDetailObj();
        INSObj.Invoice = new Object();
        INSObj.Invoice = GetProInsInvoiceObjCash();

        return INSObj;

    }

            $("#ddl_PatientCategory").disable();
