                                @*else if (objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile.ProfilePrefix == '@ViewBag.DepartmentPrefix' && objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile.ProfilePrefix === "IP") {

            let isFounded = false;
            let deptLst = [];
            if (lstOfCopayDetail != null && obj[i].DepartmentId !== undefined && obj[i].DepartmentId !== '') {
                // Convert comma-separated DepartmentId string to a list of numbers
                deptLst = obj[i].DepartmentId.split(',').map(Number);

                for (let j = 0; j < lstOfCopayDetail.length; j++) {
                    // Check 1: Exact match with DepartmentId, SectionId, and ServiceId
                    for (let k = 0; k < deptLst.length; k++) {
                        if (
                            lstOfCopayDetail[j].DepartmentId == deptLst[k] &&
                            lstOfCopayDetail[j].SectionId == obj[i].SectionId &&
                            lstOfCopayDetail[j].ServiceId == obj[i].ServiceId
                        ) {
                            CopayPer = lstOfCopayDetail[j].Copay;
                            isFounded = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }

                    // Check 2: Match DepartmentId and SectionId
                    if (!isFounded) {
                        for (let k = 0; k < deptLst.length; k++) {
                            if (
                                lstOfCopayDetail[j].DepartmentId == deptLst[k] &&
                                lstOfCopayDetail[j].SectionId == obj[i].SectionId
                            ) {
                                CopayPer = lstOfCopayDetail[j].Copay;
                                isFounded = true;
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    // Check 3: Match DepartmentId only
                    if (!isFounded) {
                        for (let k = 0; k < deptLst.length; k++) {
                            if (lstOfCopayDetail[j].DepartmentId == deptLst[k]) {
                                CopayPer = lstOfCopayDetail[j].Copay;
                                isFounded = true;
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    if (isFounded) {
                        break; // Stop looping once found
                    }
                }
            }
            let Copay = 0;

            // Make sure CopayPer is a valid number and not 0
            if (!isNaN(CopayPer) && CopayPer > 0) {
                Copay = (Inusranceprice / 100) * CopayPer;
                Copay = Copay.toFixed(2);
            } else {
                Copay = 0; // fallback value or you can set to null or a default percentage
            }

            var CopayPercentage = "";
            //if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_APPROVED || obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_REJECTED) {

            CopayPercentage = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +
                "<input id='txtRadCopayPercentage" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "' class='form-control' type='text' " +
                "oninput='RadCalculateCopayAmount(" + i + ", \"" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\", " + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", this.value)' " +

            //}
            //else {
            //    CopayPercentage = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +
            //        " <input id =\"txtRadCopayPercentage" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled  type='text' onchange = RadCalculateCopayAmount('" + obj[i].ServiceId + "',this.value);   value='" + CopayPer + "' /></td>";

            //}



            var CopayPrice = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +
                " <input id =\"txtRadCopay" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled  type='text'   value='" + Copay + "' /></td>";

            var DeductiblePrice = "";

            //if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_APPROVED || obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_REJECTED) {
            DeductiblePrice = "<td style='width:8%;display:none;'>" +
                "<input id='txtRadDeductible" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "' class='form-control' type='text' " +
                "oninput='RadCalculateDeductiblePrice(" + i + ", \"" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\", " + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", this.value)' " +
                "value='" + Deductible + "' /></td>";

            //}
            //else {
            //    DeductiblePrice = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +
            //        " <input id =\"txtRadDeductible" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled  type='text'   value='" + Deductible + "' /></td>";

            //}
            let ApprovedPrice = Inusranceprice;


            var ApprovedColumn = "";
            var RejectedColumn = "";
            //if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_REJECTED) {

            ApprovedColumn = "<td style='width:8%;'>" +
                "<input id='txtRadApprovedColumn" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "' class='form-control' type='text' " +
                "oninput='RadCalculateRejectedPrice(" + i + ", \"" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\", " + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", this.value)' " +
                "value='" + ApprovedPrice + "' /></td>";

                    //}
            //else {
            //    ApprovedColumn = "<td style='width:8%;'>" +
            //        " <input id =\"txtRadApprovedColumn" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled onchange = RadCalculateRejectedPrice('" + obj[i].ServiceId + "',this.value);  type='text'   value='" + ApprovedPrice + "' /></td>";
            //}

            var RejectedColumn = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +
                " <input id =\"txtRadRejectedColumn" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled  type='text'   value='0' /></td>";
            var status = "";
            if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_PENDING) {
                status = "<td>Pending</td>";

            } else if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_APPROVED) {
                status = "<td>Approve</td>";

            } else if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_REJECTED) {
                status = "<td>Rejected</td>";

            } else if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_NOTCOVER) {
                status = "<td>Not Cover</td>";

            } else if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_CANCEL) {
                status = "<td>Cancel</td>";

            } else if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_INFORMATIONREQUIRED) {
                status = "<td>Information Required</td>";

            } else {
                status = "<td></td>";

            }
            var newRow = "<tr id='trRadOrderCPC" + i + "'>" + indexCell + cpcOldPrice + cpcSrno + cpcName + Quantity + Instruction + cpcPrice + insPrice + InsuranceDiscountPer + InsuranceDiscountPrice + ApprovedColumn + CopayPercentage + CopayPrice + DeductiblePrice + RejectedColumn  + status + insuranceCheckbox + cashCheckbox + "</tr>";

            $("#RadOrderDetail").append(newRow);
            //if (isNaN(obj[i].PatientOrderId)) {
            //    ProHandlePaymentSelection(i, obj[i].ServiceId, JSON.stringify(obj[i]),"cash")
            //}
        }
    }
    function UpdateRadQuantity(i) {
        var quantityValue = $("#RadQuantity" + i).val();
        quantityValue = Math.max(1, parseInt(quantityValue, 10));
        selectedRadCPTs[i].Quantity = quantityValue;

        console.log("Updated Quantity for Service ID " + selectedRadCPTs[i].ServiceId + ": " + selectedRadCPTs[i].Quantity);
    }


     function DeleteCPCOrderGrid(index) {


     debugger;
         if ($("#txtReceiptVoucherId").getValue() != "") {
             var getServicePrice = new Number($("#txtRadModePrice" + selectedRadCPTs[index].ServiceId + "_" + index).getValue());
         // var payAbleAmount = new Number($("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue());
         var balanceAmount = new Number($("#txtRadBalance").getValue());
         var disc = new Number($("#txtRadDiscountPer").getValue());
         var disAmount = Math.round((getServicePrice / 100) * disc);
         getServicePrice = getServicePrice - disAmount;
         //var remainingAmount = payAbleAmount - getServicePrice;
         // var totalRecieved = new Number($("#txtRadPaidAmount").getValue());
         //if (remainingAmount < totalRecieved) {
         if (balanceAmount < getServicePrice) {
             ShowMessage('1', 'can not be delete this record,please refund.');
             return;
         }
     }


     isEdit = false;
     var GrandTotal = 0;
     //////////////
     if (selectedRadCPTs[index].Price != undefined) {
         GrandTotal = new Number(RadTotalAmount) - selectedRadCPTs[index].Price;
     }

     selectedRadCPTs.splice(index, 1);
     GrandTotal = GetRadTotalPrice();

     FillRadOrderCPCTable(selectedRadCPTs);

     if (GrandTotal != 0) {
         RadTotalAmount = GrandTotal;

         $("#txtRadTotalAmount").setValue(GrandTotal);

         $("#txtRadTotal").empty();
         $("#txtRadTotal").append("Total Price = " + GrandTotal + "\tPKR");
         $("#txtTotalTest").empty();
         $("#txtTotalTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedRadCPTs.length + "");
         $("#txtRadDiscountNet").trigger("onchange");
     }
     else {
         if (selectedRadCPTs.length == 0) {
             RadTotalAmount = GrandTotal;


             $("#txtRadTotalAmount").setValue(GrandTotal);

             $("#txtRadTotal").empty();
             $("#txtRadTotal").append("Total Price = " + GrandTotal + "\tPKR");
             $("#txtTotalTest").empty();
             $("#txtTotalTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedRadCPTs.length + "");
            // $("#txtRadDiscountPer").trigger("onkeyup");// added by saqib
             $("#txtRadDiscountNet").trigger("onchange");
         }
     }
     $("#txtTotalTest").empty();
     $("#txtTotalTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedRadCPTs.length + "");

     $("#txtRadRefundBalance").setValue(0);
     @*if ('@ViewBag.IsRecieveAmount' == 'False' || $("#txtPatientAdmitId").getValue() != "")
         $("#txtRadPaidAmount").setValue(0);*@
 }


    function RadPaymentModeChangeEvent() {
        debugger
        value = $("#ddl_RadPaymode").getValue();
        if (value != "") {
            if (PaymentModeList.length > 0 && $.isArray(PaymentModeList) != null) {
                var PaymentModeObject = $.grep(PaymentModeList, function (item) {
                    return item.ProfileId.toString() === value;
                })[0];
                if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PATPMD') {
                    $("#divRadPatientAdvance").show();
                }
                else {
                    $("#divRadPatientAdvance").hide();
                }
                if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PARPMD') {
                    $("#divRadCashReceived").show();
                    $("#divRadCreditCardReceived").show();
                    $("#divRadPatientAccountReceived").show();
                    $("#divRadPatientAdvance").show();
                    $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").disable();
                    let ReceivedAmmount = $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").getValue();

                    let CashReceived = $("#txtRadCashReceived").getValue();

                    if (CashReceived == "")
                        CashReceived = 0;
                    let CreditCardReceived = $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").getValue();
                    if (CreditCardReceived == "")
                        CreditCardReceived = 0;
                    let PatientAccountReceived = $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
                    if (PatientAccountReceived == "")
                        PatientAccountReceived = 0;
                    $("#txtRadCashReceived").setValue(ReceivedAmmount - CreditCardReceived - PatientAccountReceived);
                    $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").setValue(CreditCardReceived);
                    $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").setValue(PatientAccountReceived);


                }
                else {
                    $("#divRAdCashReceived").hide();
                    $("#divRAdCreditCardReceived").hide();
                    $("#divRAdPatientAccountReceived").hide();
                    $("#txtRadCashReceived").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                    $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").enable();
                    if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PATPMD') {
                        $("#divRadPatientAdvance").show();
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#divRadPatientAdvance").hide();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }



    function RadHandlePaymentSelection(rowNo, serviceId, seviceObj, type) {


        var RadInsuranceCheckbox = document.getElementById("RadInsurance" + rowNo);
        var RadCashCheckbox = document.getElementById("RadCash" + rowNo);

        if (type === "insurance") {
            if (RadInsuranceCheckbox.checked) {
                RadCashCheckbox.checked = false; // Uncheck Cash if Insurance is checked
                RadRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
                var RadObjIns = new Object();
                RadObjIns.ServiceId = serviceId;
                RadObjIns.IndexNo = rowNo;
                RadObjIns.Quantity = $("#txtRadQuantity" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjIns.Instruction = $("#txtRadInstruction" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjIns.NORPRC = $("#txtRadModeInsPrice" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjIns.CopayPer = $("#txtRadCopayPercentage" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjIns.Copay = $("#txtRadCopay" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjIns.InsuranceDiscPer = $("#txtRadInsuranceDiscountPer" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjIns.InsuranceDiscAmount = $("#txtRadInsuranceDiscountPrice" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjIns.Deductible = $("#txtRadDeductible" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjIns.ApprovedPrice = $("#txtRadApprovedColumn" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjIns.RejectedPrice = $("#txtRadRejectedColumn" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjIns.IsInsuranceClaim = true;
                RadObjIns.PatientPrescribeLabTestId = seviceObj.PatientPrescribeLabTestId;
                RadObjIns.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId = seviceObj.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId;

                RadInsuranceArray.push(RadObjIns); // Add to Insurance array
            } else {
                RadRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
            }
        } else if (type === "cash") {
            if (RadCashCheckbox.checked) {
                RadInsuranceCheckbox.checked = false; // Uncheck Insurance if Cash is checked
                RadRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
                var RadObjCash = new Object();
                RadObjCash.IndexNo = rowNo;
                RadObjCash.ServiceId = serviceId;
                RadObjCash.Quantity = $("#txtRadQuantity" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjCash.Instruction = $("#txtRadInstruction" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjCash.NORPRC = $("#txtRadModePrice" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
                RadObjCash.IsInsuranceClaim = false;
                RadObjCash.PatientPrescribeLabTestId = seviceObj.PatientPrescribeLabTestId;
                RadObjCash.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId = seviceObj.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId;
                RadCashArray.push(RadObjCash); // Add to Cash array
            } else {
                RadRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
            }
        }
        RadUpdateInvoiceAmounts();
        CalculateGrandTotal();
    }


    function RadRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo) {
        RadCashArray = RadCashArray.filter(item => !(item.ServiceId == serviceId && item.IndexNo == rowNo));
        RadInsuranceArray = RadInsuranceArray.filter(item => !(item.ServiceId == serviceId && item.IndexNo == rowNo));


        //RadCashArray = RadCashArray.filter(item => item.ServiceId != serviceId);
        //RadInsuranceArray = RadInsuranceArray.filter(item => item.ServiceId != serviceId);
    }




    function RadUpdateInvoiceAmounts() {
        var cashTotal = RadCashArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.NORPRC * item.Quantity), 0);
        var insuranceTotal = RadInsuranceArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.NORPRC * item.Quantity), 0);
        var totalCopay = RadInsuranceArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + ((item.Copay * 1) + (item.Deductible * 1) + (item.RejectedPrice * 1)), 0);
        var totalTotalInsuranceDiscAmount = RadInsuranceArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + ((item.InsuranceDiscAmount * 1)), 0);
        $("#txtRadTotalAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
        $("#txtRadPayableAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
        $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
        $("#txtRadPaidAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
        $("#txtRadBalance").setValue(0);
        $("#txtRadTotalRecievedAmount").setValue(cashTotal);

        $("#InsuranceRadtxtTotalAmount").setValue(insuranceTotal);
        $("#InsuranceRadTotalCopay").setValue(totalCopay.toFixed(2));

        $("#InsuranceRadtxtInsuranceDiscountAmount").setValue(totalTotalInsuranceDiscAmount.toFixed(2));
        $("#InsuranceRadtxtPayableByInsurance").setValue(insuranceTotal - totalTotalInsuranceDiscAmount - totalCopay);
        if (cashTotal == 0) {
            $("#txtRadDiscountNet").setValue(cashTotal);
        }
        $("#txtRadDiscountNet").trigger("change");


    }

    function RadfilterByCPCCode(val, e) {
        $(document).unbind("keydown");
        filteredCPTArray = new Array();
        $("#tblCPT").hide();
        $("#tblReferrals").hide();
        $("#tblReferralCodes").hide();
        $("#tblCPCCode").hide();
        if (val.trim() === "") {
            $("#tblCPCCode").hide();
            return;
        }
        //$("#tblReferrals").show();
        var dataw = filterArray(val, FilterGenderCPT);
        //filteredCPTArray = GetCPTFilterObjectArray(dataw);
        $("#tblCPCCode").show();
        var tbody = '';

        var tbody = '';
        tbody = GetCPTFilterTable(dataw);

        //if (e.keyCode == 13 && temp.length == 1) {
        //    searchByCode(temp[0].filterColumn);
        //}
        // SEARCHING PERFOME ON ENTER PRESS.
        if (e.keyCode == 13) {
            searchByCode(temp[0]);
        }

        //added by haroon 12/22/2014
        if (e.keyCode === 27) {
            $("#tblCPCCode").hide();

        }
        //end
        if (tbody.trim() == '') {
            $("#tblCPCCode").hide();
            $(document).unbind("keydown");
        }
        else {
            BindTblCPTArrowKeys("tblCPCCode", "txtCPTCode", "searchByCode");
        }

        $("#tblCPCCode").html(tbody);
    }


    function CalculateRadNetDiscount(val) {
        debugger
        /* var price = $("#txtRadTotalAmount").getValue();*/
        RadChangePrice = "True";
        var price = GetRadTotalPrice();
        $("#txtRadTotalAmount").setValue(price);
        var balance = $("#txtRadBalance").getValue();

        var disc = new Number(val);
        var paid = Math.floor(price - disc);
        //if (locationType == LOC_LABORATORY && patientType != PATTYPE_COMPANY)
        //    if (!ValidateDiscount(price, allowedDiscount, "net", disc)) {
        //        $("#txtRadDiscountNet").focus();
        //        return;
        //    }


        if (price < disc) {
            ShowMessage('1', "You can maximum give discount Rs." + Math.floor(new Number(price)));
            $("#txtRadDiscountNet").focus();
            validDiscount = false;
            return;
        }

        var perDisc = (disc / price) * 100;


        if (isNaN(perDisc)) {
            $("#txtRadDiscountPer").setValue(0);
        }
        else {
            $("#txtRadDiscountPer").setValue(new Number(perDisc).toFixed(2));
        }


        let CashReceived = $("#txtRadCashReceived").getValue();

        if (CashReceived == "")
            CashReceived = 0;
        let CreditCardReceived = $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").getValue();
        if (CreditCardReceived == "")
            CreditCardReceived = 0;
        let PatientAccountReceived = $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
        if (PatientAccountReceived == "")
            PatientAccountReceived = 0;

        $("#txtRadPayableAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - disc));
        $("#txtRadPaidAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - disc));
        $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - disc));
        debugger
        value = $("#ddl_RadPaymode").getValue();
        if (value != "") {
            if (PaymentModeList.length > 0 && $.isArray(PaymentModeList) != null) {
                var PaymentModeObject = $.grep(PaymentModeList, function (item) {
                    return item.ProfileId.toString() === value;
                })[0];
                if (RadChangePrice == "True") {
                    if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PARPMD') {
                        $("#txtRadCashReceived").setValue(price - disc);
                        $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                        $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#txtRadCashReceived").setValue(0);
                        $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                        $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                    }
                    RadChangePrice = "False";
                }
                else {
                    if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PARPMD') {

                        $("#txtRadCashReceived").setValue(Math.floor(price - CreditCardReceived - PatientAccountReceived - disAmount));
                        $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").setValue(CreditCardReceived);
                        $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").setValue(PatientAccountReceived);
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#txtRadCashReceived").setValue(0);
                        $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                        $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        $("#txtRadTotalRecievedAmount").setValue($("#txtRadPayableAmount").val());

        CalculateRadRemainingAmount();


    }
    function GetRadTotalPrice() {
        debugger
        var getTotalPrice = 0;
        //var getInsuraceTotalPrice = 0
        try {
            if (RadCashArray != null) {
                for (var i = 0; i < RadCashArray.length; i++) {
                    var getPrice = $("#txtRadModePrice" + RadCashArray[i].ServiceId + "_" + RadCashArray[i].IndexNo).getValue();
                    //if (RadCashArray[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == 2) {
                    //    if (getPrice == "")
                    //        getPrice = 0;
                    //    getInsuraceTotalPrice = new Number(getInsuraceTotalPrice) + new Number(getPrice);
                    //}

                    if (getPrice == "")
                        getPrice = 0;
                    getTotalPrice = new Number(getTotalPrice) + new Number(getPrice);


                }
                //$("#txtPayableByInsurance").setValue(getInsuraceTotalPrice);
            }
            return getTotalPrice;
        } catch (e) {
            console.log(e.message);
        }
    }
    function CalculateRadPerDiscount(val) {
        //var price = $("#txtRadTotalAmount").getValue();


        var price = GetRadTotalPrice();
        /*var price = 0;*/
        $("#txtRadTotalAmount").setValue(price);


        var balance = $("#txtRadBalance").getValue();


        var disc = new Number(val);
        var disAmount = Math.round((price / 100) * disc);
        var paid = Math.floor(price - disAmount);
        var dis = $("#txtRadDiscountNet").getValue();
        //if (locationType == LOC_LABORATORY && patientType != PATTYPE_COMPANY)
        //    if (!ValidateDiscount(price, allowedDiscount, "per", disc)) {
        //        $("#txtRadDiscountPer").focus();
        //        return;
        //    }

        if (disc > 100) {
            ShowMessage('1', "Invalid discount");
            $("#txtRadDiscountPer").focus();
            validDiscount = false;
            return;
        }
        $("#txtRadPayableAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - dis));
        $("#txtRadPaidAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - dis));
        $("#txtRadCashReceived").setValue(Math.floor(price - dis));
        $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
        $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
        @*if ('@ViewBag.labId' != '') // saqib
            $("#txtRadReceived").setValue(Math.floor(price - disAmount)); // saqib discount*@
        $("#txtRadTotalRecievedAmount").setValue($("#txtRadReceived").val()); // saqib discount


        //var netDisc = (val / 100) * price;

        //$("#txtRadDiscountNet").setValue(Math.round(netDisc));

        CalculateRadRemainingAmount();

    }
    function CalculateRadCurrentRemainingAmount() {
        var currentrecived = $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").getValue();
        var payedAmount = $("#txtRadPaidAmount").getValue();
        var payAbleAmount = $("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue();
        var netRecieved = $("#txtRadReceived").getValue();

        var dueRecived = $("#txtRadDueRecieved").getValue();


        var balanceAmount = new Number(netRecieved) + new Number(currentrecived) - new Number(dueRecived);
        balanceAmount = (new Number($("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue())) - (new Number($("#txtRadReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadCurrentAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadReturn").getValue()));//new Number(payAbleAmount) - balanceAmount;

        if (balanceAmount < 0) {
            ShowMessage('1', MSG_BALANCE);
            $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").setValue(0);
            $("#txtRadPaidAmount").setValue(0);

            $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").focus();
            $("#txtRadBalance").setValue((new Number($("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue())) - (new Number($("#txtRadReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadCurrentAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadReturn").getValue())));

            return false;
        }
        var totalRecievedAmount = new Number(netRecieved) + new Number(currentrecived);
        $("#txtRadBalance").setValue(new Number($("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue()) - (new Number($("#txtRadTotalRecievedAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadCurrentAmount").getValue())));

        $("#txtRadPaidAmount").setValue(new Number($("#txtRadReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadCurrentAmount").getValue()));
        $("#txtRadTotalRecievedAmount").setValue(new Number($("#txtRadReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadDueRecieved").getValue()));
        $("#txtRadBalance").setValue((new Number($("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue())) - (new Number($("#txtRadReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadCurrentAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtRadReturn").getValue())));

        return true;
    }
    function CalculateRadParitalReceivedAmount() {
        debugger
        $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").setValue(0);
        var CashAmount = $("#txtRadCashReceived").getValue();
        var CreditAmount = $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").getValue();
        var PatientAmount = $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
        var RadTotalAmount = new Number(CashAmount) + new Number(CreditAmount) + new Number(PatientAmount);
        $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").setValue(RadTotalAmount);
        CalculateRadCurrentRemainingAmount();
    }
    function CalculateRadRemainingAmount() {
        debugger
        var payedAmount = $("#txtRadPaidAmount").getValue();
        var payAbleAmount = $("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue();
        var netRecieved = $("#txtRadReceived").getValue();
        var dueRecieved = $("#txtRadDueRecieved").getValue();


        var currentRecived = new Number($("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue()) - new Number($("#txtRadTotalRecievedAmount").getValue());


        debugger
        var balanceAmount = new Number($("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue()) - (new Number($("#txtRadTotalRecievedAmount").getValue()));
        $("#txtRadPaidAmount").setValue(new Number($("#txtRadTotalRecievedAmount").getValue()));
        if (balanceAmount < 0) {
            ShowMessage('1', MSG_BALANCE);
            $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").setValue(0);
            $("#txtRadPaidAmount").setValue(0);
            $("#txtRadCurrentAmount").focus();
            return false;
        }

        $("#txtRadBalance").setValue(balanceAmount);

        return true;
    }




    function RadChangePriceMode(id, price, e) {
        var priceMode = "NORPRC";
        RadTotalAmount = 0;
        RadChangePrice = "True";
        var found = false;
        for (var j = 0; j < selectedRadCPTs.length; j++) {
            if (id == selectedRadCPTs[j].ServiceId) {


                selectedRadCPTs[j].ServicePriceModePrefix = "NORPRC";
                selectedRadCPTs[j].Price = price;
                selectedRadCPTs[j].NORPRC = price;
                selectedRadCPTs[j].PriceForEdit = price;

                for (var k = 0; k < lstPriceMode.length; k++) {
                    if (lstPriceMode[k].ProfilePrefix == priceMode) {
                        selectedRadCPTs[j].ServicePriceModeId = lstPriceMode[k].ProfileId;
                    }
                }
            }
            if (selectedRadCPTs[j].Price != undefined) {
                RadTotalAmount = new Number(RadTotalAmount) + new Number(selectedRadCPTs[j].Price);
            }
        }
        RadTotalAmount = GetRadTotalPrice();
        //RadTotalAmount = 0;
        if (RadTotalAmount != 0) {
            $("#txtRadTotalAmount").setValue(RadTotalAmount);
            $("#txtRadPayableAmount").setValue(RadTotalAmount);
            $("#txtRadBalance").setValue(RadTotalAmount);
            // $("#txtRadPaidAmount").setValue(RadTotalAmount); //saqib

            $("#txtRadTotal").empty();
            $("#txtRadTotal").append("Total Price = " + RadTotalAmount + "\tPKR");
            $("#txtTotalTest").empty();
            $("#txtTotalTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedRadCPTs.length + "");
            $("#txtRadDiscountNet").trigger("onchange");

            //CalculateRadPerDiscount($("#txtRadDiscountPer").getValue());

        }
        $("#txtTotalTest").empty();
        $("#txtTotalTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedRadCPTs.length + "");
    }



    function GetRadInvoiceObjCash() {

        try {
            var objVoucher = new Object();
            objVoucher.PayModeProfileId = $("#ddl_RadPaymode").getValue();
            var objInvoice = new Object();

            objInvoice.InvoiceId = $("#txtRadInvoiceId").getValue();
            objInvoice.VoucherId = $("#txtRadVoucherId").getValue();
            objInvoice.ReceiptVoucherId = $("#txtRadReceiptVoucherId").getValue();
            objInvoice.CashReceived = $("#txtRadCashReceived").getValue();
            objInvoice.CreditCardReceived = $("#txtRadCreditCardReceived").getValue();
            objInvoice.PatientAccountReceived = $("#txtRadPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
            objInvoice.TotalReceived = $("#txtRadPaidAmount").getValue();

            objVoucher.VoucherId = $("#txtRadVoucherReceiptId").getValue();
            objVoucher.TotalCredit = objInvoice.TotalReceived;
            objVoucher.TotalDebit = objInvoice.TotalReceived;

            objInvoice.Voucher1 = objVoucher;

            return objInvoice;
        } catch (e) {

        }

    }

    function GetRadCashOrderDetailObj() {
        var RadTotalAmount = $("#txtRadTotalAmount").getValue();
        var discountNet = $("#txtRadDiscountNet").getValue();
        var discPer = $("#txtRadDiscountPer").getValue();
        var payAmount = $("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue();

        var payMode = $("#ddl_RadPaymode").getValue();

        var paidAmount = $("#txtRadPaidAmount").getValue();
        var balance = $("#txtRadBalance").getValue();
        var miscAmount = 0;
        var tax = 0;

        let profilePrefix = "";

        var ServicePackageId = 0;
        var lstCashOrderDetail = new Array();

        var lineID = 1;

        for (var i = 0; i < RadCashArray.length; i++) {
            debugger
            var cpcDiscount = 0;
            var grossAmount = 0;
            var amount = 0;

            var objCashOrdDetail = new Object();
            if (RadCashArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId != null) {
                objCashOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = RadCashArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
            }
            objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailSet = new Object();
            if (RadCashArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId != undefined) {
                objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = RadCashArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId;

            }
            else {
                objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = 0;
            }

            if (profilePrefix != "GRTPAT") {
                if (RadCashArray[i].ServicePackageId == undefined) {
                    if (objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                        if (RadCashArray[i].PriceForEdit == 0) {
                            ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (RadCashArray[i].NORPRC != undefined)
                            if (RadCashArray[i].NORPRC == 0) {
                                ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                                return;
                            }
                    }
                }
            }

            objCashOrdDetail.DiscPercent = discPer;

            if (RadCashArray[i].ServicePackageId != undefined) {
                ServicePackageId = RadCashArray[i].ServicePackageId;
                objCashOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = RadCashArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
            }
            objCashOrdDetail.PriceModeProfileId = RadCashArray[i].ServicePriceModeId;

            objCashOrdDetail.ServiceId = RadCashArray[i].ServiceId
            objCashOrdDetail.PatientPrescribeLabTestId = RadCashArray[i].PatientPrescribeLabTestId;
            objCashOrdDetail.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId = RadCashArray[i].PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId;

            if (RadCashArray[i].IsSTAT) {
                cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(RadTotalAmount, RadCashArray[i].STATPrice, discountNet);
                grossAmount = new Number(RadCashArray[i].STATPrice) - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                amount = RadCashArray[i].STATPrice;
            }
            else {
                if (objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                    cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(RadTotalAmount, RadCashArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                    grossAmount = new Number(RadCashArray[i].NORPRC) - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                    amount = RadCashArray[i].NORPRC;
                }
                else {
                    cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(RadTotalAmount, RadCashArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                    grossAmount = new Number(RadCashArray[i].NORPRC) - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                    amount = RadCashArray[i].NORPRC;
                }


            }
            objCashOrdDetail.IsInsuranceClaim = RadCashArray[i].IsInsuranceClaim;
            objCashOrdDetail.Amount = amount;
            objCashOrdDetail.Price = amount;
            objCashOrdDetail.Quantity = RadCashArray[i].Quantity || 1;
            //objCashOrdDetail.Quantity = Quantity;
            objCashOrdDetail.DiscPerUnit = cpcDiscount;
            objCashOrdDetail.DiscountAmount = cpcDiscount;
            objCashOrdDetail.GrossAmount = grossAmount;

            objCashOrdDetail.MiscPerUnit = 0;
            objCashOrdDetail.MiscAmount = 0;
            objCashOrdDetail.NetAmount = grossAmount;
            objCashOrdDetail.NetPrice = grossAmount;
            objCashOrdDetail.ReceivableAmount = grossAmount;
            objCashOrdDetail.TaxAmount = 0;
            objCashOrdDetail.TaxPercent = 0;
            objCashOrdDetail.LineDescription = RadCashArray[i].Remarks;

            objCashOrdDetail.ReportDateTime = RadCashArray[i].ReportDateTime;
            objCashOrdDetail.IsSampleBrought = RadCashArray[i].IsSampleBrought;
            lstCashOrderDetail.push(objCashOrdDetail);
            lineID++;
        }

        return lstCashOrderDetail;
    }

    function GetRadINSOrderDetailObj() {

        let profilePrefix = "";

        var ServicePackageId = 0;
        let discountNet = 0;
        let RadTotalAmount = $("#InsuranceRadtxtTotalAmount").getValue();
        var lstInsOrderDetail = new Array();
        let lineID = 1;
        for (var i = 0; i < RadInsuranceArray.length; i++) {
            debugger
            var cpcDiscount = 0;
            var grossAmount = 0;
            var amount = 0;
            var objINSOrdDetail = new Object();
            if (RadInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId != null) {
                objINSOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = RadInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
            }
            objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailSet = new Object();
            if (RadInsuranceArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId != undefined) {
                objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = RadInsuranceArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId;
            }
            else {
                objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = 0;
            }
            if (profilePrefix != "GRTPAT") {
                if (RadInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageId == undefined) {
                    if (objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                        if (RadInsuranceArray[i].PriceForEdit == 0) {
                            ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (RadInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC != undefined)
                            if (RadInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC == 0) {
                                ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                                return;
                            }
                    }
                }
            }

            objINSOrdDetail.DiscPercent = 0;
            if (RadInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageId != undefined) {
                ServicePackageId = RadInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageId;
                objINSOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = RadInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
            }
            objINSOrdDetail.PriceModeProfileId = RadInsuranceArray[i].ServicePriceModeId;

            objINSOrdDetail.ServiceId = RadInsuranceArray[i].ServiceId
            objINSOrdDetail.PatientPrescribeLabTestId = RadInsuranceArray[i].PatientPrescribeLabTestId;
            objINSOrdDetail.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId = RadInsuranceArray[i].PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId;

            if (RadInsuranceArray[i].IsSTAT) {
                cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(RadTotalAmount, RadInsuranceArray[i].STATPrice, discountNet);
                grossAmount = new Number(RadInsuranceArray[i].STATPrice); //- new Number(cpcDiscount);
                amount = RadInsuranceArray[i].STATPrice;
            }
            else {
                if (objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                    cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(RadTotalAmount, RadInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                    grossAmount = new Number(RadInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC);// - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                    amount = RadInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC;
                }
                else {
                    cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(RadTotalAmount, RadInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                    grossAmount = new Number(RadInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC);// - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                    amount = RadInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC;
                }
            }

            objINSOrdDetail.IsInsuranceClaim = RadInsuranceArray[i].IsInsuranceClaim;
            objINSOrdDetail.Amount = amount;
            objINSOrdDetail.Price = (RadInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (RadInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (RadInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
            objINSOrdDetail.CopayPer = RadInsuranceArray[i].CopayPer;
            objINSOrdDetail.Copay = RadInsuranceArray[i].Copay;
            objINSOrdDetail.Deductible = RadInsuranceArray[i].Deductible;
            objINSOrdDetail.ApprovedPrice = RadInsuranceArray[i].ApprovedPrice;
            objINSOrdDetail.RejectedPrice = RadInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice;
            objINSOrdDetail.InsuranceDiscPer = RadInsuranceArray[i].InsuranceDiscPer;
            objINSOrdDetail.InsuranceDiscAmount = RadInsuranceArray[i].InsuranceDiscAmount;
            objINSOrdDetail.Quantity = RadInsuranceArray[i].Quantity || 1;
            objINSOrdDetail.DiscPerUnit = cpcDiscount;
            objINSOrdDetail.DiscountAmount = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.GrossAmount = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.MiscPerUnit = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.MiscAmount = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.NetAmount = (RadInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (RadInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (RadInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
            objINSOrdDetail.NetPrice = (RadInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (RadInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (RadInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
            objINSOrdDetail.ReceivableAmount = (RadInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (RadInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (RadInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
            objINSOrdDetail.TaxAmount = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.TaxPercent = 0;
            objINSOrdDetail.LineDescription = RadInsuranceArray[i].Remarks;
            objINSOrdDetail.ReportDateTime = RadInsuranceArray[i].ReportDateTime;
            objINSOrdDetail.IsSampleBrought = RadInsuranceArray[i].IsSampleBrought;
            lstInsOrderDetail.push(objINSOrdDetail);
            lineID++;
        }

        return lstInsOrderDetail;
    }

    }

    function GetRadPatientOrderObjForCash() {
        debugger
        var RadTotalAmount = $("#txtRadTotalAmount").getValue();
        var discountNet = $("#txtRadDiscountNet").getValue();
        var discPer = $("#txtRadDiscountPer").getValue();
        var payAmount = $("#txtRadPayableAmount").getValue();


        var paidAmount = $("#txtRadPaidAmount").getValue();
        var balance = $("#txtRadBalance").getValue();
        var miscAmount = 0;
        var tax = 0;
        var cashObj = new Object();
        cashObj = GetPatientOrderObjData();
        cashObj.DocMovement = new Object();
        cashObj.DocMovement.ShortName = 'RIMPOD';

        cashObj.PatientOrderSet.RefPersonName = $("#txtDepartmentComponentId option:selected").text();
        cashObj.PatientOrderSet.PaymentMethodProfileId = $("#ddl_RadPaymode").getValue();
        cashObj.PatientOrderSet.PatientOrderSetId = $("#txtRadPatientOrderSetId").getValue();
        cashObj.PatientOrderId = $("#txtRadPatientOrderId").getValue();

        cashObj.InvoiceId = $("#txtRadInvoiceId").getValue();
        cashObj.PatientOrderSet.IsInsuranceOrder = false;
        cashObj.TotalAmount = Math.floor(RadTotalAmount);
        cashObj.TotalAmountDecimal = RadTotalAmount

        cashObj.TotalDiscount = discountNet;
        cashObj.TotalGross = payAmount;
        cashObj.TotalMisc = miscAmount;
        cashObj.TotalNet = payAmount;
        cashObj.TotalReceivable = payAmount;
        cashObj.TotalTax = tax;
        cashObj.DiscPercent = discPer;
        cashObj.Patient = new Object();
        cashObj.Patient = GetPatientObjData();
        cashObj.PatientOrderDetails = new Array();
        cashObj.PatientOrderDetails = GetRadCashOrderDetailObj();
        cashObj.Invoice = new Object();
        cashObj.Invoice = GetRadInvoiceObjCash();

        return cashObj;
    }



    function GetRadPatientOrderObjForInsurance() {

        debugger



        var insurancetotalAmount = $("#InsuranceRadtxtTotalAmount").getValue();
        let totalCopay = $("#InsuranceRadTotalCopay").getValue();
        var PayablebyInsurance = $("#InsuranceRadtxtPayableByInsurance").getValue();
        var insuranceDiscountAmount = $("#InsuranceLabtxtInsuranceDiscountAmount").getValue();
        var INSObj = new Object();
        INSObj = GetPatientOrderObjData();
        INSObj.DocMovement = new Object();
        INSObj.DocMovement.ShortName = 'RIMPOD';

        INSObj.PatientOrderSet.RefPersonName = $("#txtDepartmentComponentId option:selected").text();
        INSObj.PatientOrderSet.PaymentMethodProfileId = $("#ddl_InsuranceRadPaymode").getValue();
        INSObj.PatientOrderSet.PatientOrderSetId = $("#txtRadInsPatientOrderSetId").getValue();
        INSObj.PatientOrderId = $("#txtRadInsPatientOrderId").getValue();
        INSObj.PatientOrderSet.IsInsuranceOrder = true;
        INSObj.TotalAmount = Math.floor(insurancetotalAmount);
        INSObj.TotalAmountDecimal = insurancetotalAmount;
        INSObj.TotalCopay = totalCopay;
        INSObj.TotalDiscount = 0;
        INSObj.TotalGross = (totalCopay * 1);
        INSObj.TotalMisc = 0;
        INSObj.TotalNet = 0;
        INSObj.TotalReceivable = (totalCopay * 1);

        INSObj.PayableToInsurance = PayablebyInsurance;

        INSObj.InsuranceDiscountAmount = insuranceDiscountAmount;
        INSObj.TotalTax = 0;

        INSObj.Patient = new Object();
        INSObj.Patient = GetPatientObjData();

        INSObj.PatientOrderDetails = new Array();
        INSObj.PatientOrderDetails = GetRadINSOrderDetailObj();
        INSObj.Invoice = new Object();
        INSObj.Invoice = GetRadInsInvoiceObjCash();

        return INSObj;

    }

   function GetInsuranceLabData(Id) {
     debugger
     var patientOrder = new Array();
       var departmentShortName = 'PATH';

     let docMovementShortName = '@ViewBag.DocMovementShortName';
     $("#loading-image").show();

     //var _data = "{id:'" + Id + "',shortName:'" + departmentShortName + "'}";
     $.AjaxJsonAsynRequest(_url, _data, function (msg) {
         if (msg != null && msg != "[]" && msg != "") {
             debugger
             ////GetAllCPCbyPatientCategory(175, null, '@ViewBag.department', '');
             patientOrder = $.parseJSON(msg);

             var e = jQuery.Event("keypress");
             e.keyCode = $.ui.keyCode.ENTER;
             //var actualDate = patientOrder[0].DOB;
             //debugger
             //var d = new Date(patientOrder[0].DOB);
             //var dt = ('0' + d.getDate()).slice(-2) + "/" + ('0' + (d.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "/" + d.getFullYear();
             //$('#dpkDOB').val(dt);
             //CalculateAge();
             var actualDate = patientOrder[0].DOB;
             //$("#dpkDOB").setValue(ConvertToMonthDayYearFormatRe(new Date(parseInt(patientOrder[0].DOB.substr(6)))));
             debugger
             var d = new Date(patientOrder[0].DOB);
             var dt = ('0' + d.getDate()).slice(-2) + "/" + ('0' + (d.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "/" + d.getFullYear();
             $('#dpkDOB').val(ConvertToMonthDayYearFormatRe(new Date(patientOrder[0].DOB)));
             CalculateAge();
             $("#txtPatientVisitId").setValue(patientOrder[0].PatientVisitId);


             $("#txtLabInvoiceId").setValue("");
             $("#txtLabInsInvoiceId").setValue("");


             debugger
             $("#txtPatientAdmitId").setValue(patientOrder[0].PatientAdmitId);
             if (patientOrder[0].PartyName != '') {
                 $("#txtInsuranceCompanyName").setValue(patientOrder[0].PartyName);
                 $("#txtInsuranceCompanyId").setValue(patientOrder[0].InsuranceCompanyId);
             }
             if (patientOrder[0].PackageName != '') {
                 $("#txtPacakgeName").setValue(patientOrder[0].PackageName);
                 $("#txtInsurancePackageId").setValue(patientOrder[0].InsurancePackageId);
                 $("#txtPolicyNo").setValue(patientOrder[0].PolicyNo);
             }
               if ('@ViewBag.DocMovementShortName' != "CLNPOD") {
                $("#txtConsultant").setValue(patientOrder[0].EmployeeName);
            $("#txtConsultant").disable();
  }
             selectedLabCPTs = patientOrder;
             FillLabOrderCPCTable(selectedLabCPTs);

             LabPaymentModeChangeEvent();

         }
     });
    }



       function FillLabOrderCPCTable(obj) {
       debugger;
       isCheckZero = true;
       ClearGrid($("#tblLabOrderCPC tr").length, "trLabOrderCPC");

       if (obj.length == 0) {
           $("#ddl_PatientCategory").enable();
           $("#txtLabTotalAmount").setValue(0);
           $("#txtLabDiscountNet").setValue(0);
           $("#txtLabDiscountPer").setValue(0);
           $("#txtLabPayableAmount").setValue(0);
           $("#txtLabPaidAmount").setValue(0);
           $("#txtLabBalance").setValue(0);
           return;
       } else {
           $("#ddl_PatientCategory").disable();
       }


                let CopayPer = 0;
                let Deductible = 0;
           debugger
           if ('@ViewBag.DocMovementShortName' == "CLNPOD") {
               if (objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail != null) {

                   for (var i = 0; i < objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail.length; i++) {
                       if (objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile != null) {

                           if (objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile.ProfilePrefix == '@ViewBag.DepartmentPrefix' && objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile.ProfilePrefix === "DNTL") {
                               CopayPer = objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].CoInsurance;
                           }
                           else if ('@ViewBag.DepartmentPrefix' == "Gyne" && objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile.ProfilePrefix === "CLNPOD") {
                                CopayPer = objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].CoInsurance;
                            }
                           else if ('@ViewBag.DepartmentPrefix' != "DNTL" && '@ViewBag.DepartmentPrefix' != "Gyne" && objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile.ProfilePrefix === "CLNPOD") {
                               CopayPer = objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].CoInsurance;
                           }

                           @*else if (objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile.ProfilePrefix == '@ViewBag.DepartmentPrefix' && objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile.ProfilePrefix === "IP") {
                               CopayPer = objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].CoInsurance;
                           }*@
                       }

                   }
               }
           }
           else {
               if (objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail != null) {

                   for (var i = 0; i < objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail.length; i++) {
                       if (objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile != null) {

                           if (objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile.ProfilePrefix == '@ViewBag.DepartmentPrefix' && objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Profile.ProfilePrefix === "INP") {
                               CopayPer = objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].CoInsurance;
                           }
                       }
                       //if (obj.ServicePrefix?.toUpperCase() === "CONS") {
                       //    Deductible = objpatientObject.PatientInsuranceDetail[i].Deductible;
                       //}
                   }
               }
           }



       var cols = Object.getOwnPropertyNames(obj[0]).sort();

       for (var i = 0; i < obj.length; i++) {
           var found = false;
           for (var j = 0; j < selectedProcCPTs.length; j++) {
               if (selectedProcCPTs[j].ServiceId == obj[i].ServiceId) {
                   found = true;
               }
           }
           var Inusranceprice = 0;
           var price = obj[i].NORPRC;
           if (obj[i].InsurancePrice != null && obj[i].InsurancePrice != "" && obj[i].InsurancePrice != undefined)
               Inusranceprice = obj[i].InsurancePrice;
           if (obj[i].Remarks == null || obj[i].Remarks == undefined)
               obj[i].Remarks == "";

           var indexCell = "<td style='display:none'><input readonly='readonly' value='" + i + "' /></td>";
           var cpcOldPrice = "<td style='display:none'><input type='text' id='txtLabPrice" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "' class = 'form-control' disabled  /></td>";
           var cpcSrno = "<td  style='width:2%;'><input id='txtLabSrno" + i + "' class = 'form-control' disabled   type='text' value='" + (new Number(i) + new Number(1)) + "' /></td>";

           var Instruction = "<td  style='width:15%;'><input id='txtLabInstruction" + i + "' class = 'form-control' disabled   type='text' value='" + obj[i].InstructionsToReception + "' /></td>";

               "<input id='txtLabQuantity" + i + "' class='form-control' disabled type='number' value='" + (obj[i].Quantity || 1) + "' min='1' onchange='updateLabQuantity(" + i + ")' />" +
               "</td>";

           var InsuranceDiscountPer = "<td style='width:8%;display:none;'>" +

           let discountAmount = (Inusranceprice / 100) * obj[i].InsuranceDiscount;


           var InsuranceDiscountPrice = "<td style='width:8%;display:none;'>" +
               " <input id =\"txtLabInsuranceDiscountPrice" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "\" class = 'form-control'  type='text' disabled  value='" + discountAmount + "' /></td>";


           var cpcPrice = "<td style='width:8%;'>" +
               "<input id=\"txtLabModePrice" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled  type='text' onchange = LabChangePriceMode('" + obj[i].ServiceId + "',this.value); return false;' value='" + price + "' /></td>";


           var insuranceCheckbox = "";

           //    insuranceCheckbox = "<td><input class='checkbox' type='checkbox' disabled id='LabInsurance" + i + "' value='true' onclick='LabHandlePaymentSelection(" + i + ", " + obj[i].ServiceId + "," + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", \"insurance\")' /></td>";
           //}
           //else {
               insuranceCheckbox = "<td><input class='checkbox' type='checkbox' id='LabInsurance" + i + "' value='true' onclick='LabHandlePaymentSelection(" + i + ", " + obj[i].ServiceId + "," + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", \"insurance\")' /></td>";

           //}
           //else {
           //    insuranceCheckbox = "<td><input class='checkbox' type='checkbox' disabled id='LabInsurance" + i + "' value='true' onclick='LabHandlePaymentSelection(" + i + ", " + obj[i].ServiceId + "," + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", \"insurance\")' /></td>";

               cashCheckbox = "<td><input class='checkbox' type='checkbox'  id='LabCash" + i + "' value='false' onclick='LabHandlePaymentSelection(" + i + ", " + obj[i].ServiceId + "," + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", \"cash\")' /></td>";
