           //}
           //else {
           //    cashCheckbox = "<td><input class='checkbox' type='checkbox' checked id='cash" + i + "' value='true' onclick='LabHandlePaymentSelection(" + i + ", " + obj[i].ServiceId + "," + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", \"cash\")' /></td>";

           //}

           //var cpcRemove = "<td><button type='button' style=' border: none; background: transparent;'  id=\"remove" + i + "\" onclick=\"DeleteProCPCOrderGrid(" + i + ");\"><img src='/Images/Icons/Delete.png' style='width:30px;height:30px;margin-left: 12.2%;' /></button></td>";
           let isFounded = false;
           let deptLst = [];
           if (lstOfCopayDetail != null && obj[i].DepartmentId !== undefined && obj[i].DepartmentId !== '') {
               // Convert comma-separated DepartmentId string to a list of numbers
               deptLst = obj[i].DepartmentId.split(',').map(Number);

               for (let j = 0; j < lstOfCopayDetail.length; j++) {
                   // Check 1: Exact match with DepartmentId, SectionId, and ServiceId
                   for (let k = 0; k < deptLst.length; k++) {
                       if (
                           lstOfCopayDetail[j].DepartmentId == deptLst[k] &&
                           lstOfCopayDetail[j].SectionId == obj[i].SectionId &&
                           lstOfCopayDetail[j].ServiceId == obj[i].ServiceId
                       ) {
                           CopayPer = lstOfCopayDetail[j].Copay;
                           isFounded = true;
                           break;
                       }
                   }

                   // Check 2: Match DepartmentId and SectionId
                   if (!isFounded) {
                       for (let k = 0; k < deptLst.length; k++) {
                           if (
                               lstOfCopayDetail[j].DepartmentId == deptLst[k] &&
                               lstOfCopayDetail[j].SectionId == obj[i].SectionId
                           ) {
                               CopayPer = lstOfCopayDetail[j].Copay;
                               isFounded = true;
                               break;
                           }
                       }
                   }

                   // Check 3: Match DepartmentId only
                   if (!isFounded) {
                       for (let k = 0; k < deptLst.length; k++) {
                           if (lstOfCopayDetail[j].DepartmentId == deptLst[k]) {
                               CopayPer = lstOfCopayDetail[j].Copay;
                               isFounded = true;
                               break;
                           }
                       }
                   }

                   if (isFounded) {
                       break; // Stop looping once found
                   }
               }
           }
           let Copay = 0;

           // Make sure CopayPer is a valid number and not 0
           if (!isNaN(CopayPer) && CopayPer > 0) {
               Copay = (Inusranceprice / 100) * CopayPer;
               Copay = Copay.toFixed(2);
           } else {
               Copay = 0; // fallback value or you can set to null or a default percentage
           }


           var CopayPercentage = "";
           //if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_APPROVED || obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_REJECTED || obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_PENDING) {


           CopayPercentage = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +
               "<input id='txtLabCopayPercentage" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "' class='form-control' type='text' " +
               "oninput='LabCalculateCopayAmount(" + i + ", \"" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\", " + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", this.value)' " +
               "value='" + CopayPer + "' /></td>";

          //}
           //else {
           //    CopayPercentage = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +
           //        " <input id =\"txtLabCopayPercentage" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled type='text' onchange = LabCalculateCopayAmount('" + obj[i].ServiceId + "',this.value);   value='" + CopayPer + "' /></td>";

           //}



           var CopayPrice = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +
               " <input id =\"txtLabCopay" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled  type='text'   value='" + Copay + "' /></td>";

           var DeductiblePrice = "";

           //if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_APPROVED || obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_REJECTED || obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_PENDING) {

           DeductiblePrice = "<td style='width:8%;display:none;'>" +
               "<input id='txtLabDeductible" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "' class='form-control' type='text' " +
               "oninput='LabCalculateDeductiblePrice(" + i + ", \"" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\", " + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", this.value)' " +
               "value='" + Deductible + "' /></td>";


          //}
          // else {
          //      DeductiblePrice = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +
          //          " <input id =\"txtLabDeductible" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled type='text'   value='" + Deductible + "' /></td>";

          // }


           let ApprovedPrice = Inusranceprice;



           var ApprovedColumn = "";
           var RejectedColumn = "";
           /*if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_REJECTED) {*/

           ApprovedColumn = "<td style='width:8%;'>" +
               "<input id='txtLabApprovedColumn" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "' class='form-control' type='text' " +
               "oninput='LabCalculateRejectedPrice(" + i + ", \"" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\", " + JSON.stringify(obj[i]) + ", this.value)' " +
               "value='" + ApprovedPrice + "' /></td>";

          //   }
           //else {
           //     ApprovedColumn = "<td style='width:8%;'>" +
           //        " <input id =\"txtLabApprovedColumn" + obj[i].ServiceId + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled onchange = LabCalculateRejectedPrice('" + obj[i].ServiceId + "',this.value);  type='text'   value='" + ApprovedPrice + "' /></td>";
           //  }

            RejectedColumn = "<td style='width:5%;'>" +
                " <input id =\"txtLabRejectedColumn" + obj[i].ServiceId + "_" + i + "\" class = 'form-control' disabled  type='text'   value='0' /></td>";



           var status = "";
           if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_PENDING) {
               status = "<td>Pending</td>";

           } else if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_APPROVED) {
               status = "<td>Approve</td>";

           } else if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_REJECTED) {
               status = "<td>Rejected</td>";

           } else if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_NOTCOVER) {
               status = "<td>Not Cover</td>";

           } else if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_CANCEL) {
               status = "<td>Cancel</td>";

           } else if (obj[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == INS_INFORMATIONREQUIRED) {
               status = "<td>Information Required</td>";

           } else {
               status = "<td></td>";

           }

           var newRow = "<tr id='trLabOrderCPC" + i + "'>" + indexCell + cpcOldPrice + cpcSrno + cpcName + Quantity + Instruction + cpcPrice + insPrice + InsuranceDiscountPer + InsuranceDiscountPrice + ApprovedColumn + CopayPercentage + CopayPrice + DeductiblePrice + RejectedColumn + status + insuranceCheckbox + cashCheckbox + "</tr>";

           $("#LabOrderDetail").append(newRow);
           //if (isNaN(obj[i].PatientOrderId)) {
           //    ProHandlePaymentSelection(i, obj[i].ServiceId, JSON.stringify(obj[i]),"cash")
           //}
       }
   }
   function UpdateLabQuantity(i) {
       var quantityValue = $("#LabQuantity" + i).val();
       quantityValue = Math.max(1, parseInt(quantityValue, 10));
       selectedLabCPTs[i].Quantity = quantityValue;

       console.log("Updated Quantity for Service ID " + selectedLabCPTs[i].ServiceId + ": " + selectedLabCPTs[i].Quantity);
   }


    function DeleteCPCOrderGrid(index) {


    debugger;
        if ($("#txtReceiptVoucherId").getValue() != "") {
            var getServicePrice = new Number($("#txtLabModePrice" + selectedLabCPTs[index].ServiceId + "_" + index).getValue());
        // var payAbleAmount = new Number($("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue());
        var balanceAmount = new Number($("#txtLabBalance").getValue());
        var disc = new Number($("#txtLabDiscountPer").getValue());
        var disAmount = Math.round((getServicePrice / 100) * disc);
        getServicePrice = getServicePrice - disAmount;
        //var remainingAmount = payAbleAmount - getServicePrice;
        // var totalRecieved = new Number($("#txtLabPaidAmount").getValue());
        //if (remainingAmount < totalRecieved) {
        if (balanceAmount < getServicePrice) {
            ShowMessage('1', 'can not be delete this record,please refund.');
            return;
        }
    }


    isEdit = false;
    var GrandTotal = 0;
    //////////////
    if (selectedLabCPTs[index].Price != undefined) {
        GrandTotal = new Number(LabTotalAmount) - selectedLabCPTs[index].Price;
    }

    selectedLabCPTs.splice(index, 1);
    GrandTotal = GetLabTotalPrice();

    FillLabOrderCPCTable(selectedLabCPTs);

    if (GrandTotal != 0) {
        LabTotalAmount = GrandTotal;

        $("#txtLabTotalAmount").setValue(GrandTotal);

        $("#txtLabTotal").empty();
        $("#txtLabTotal").append("Total Price = " + GrandTotal + "\tPKR");
        $("#txtTotalTest").empty();
        $("#txtTotalTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedLabCPTs.length + "");
        $("#txtLabDiscountNet").trigger("onchange");
    }
    else {
        if (selectedLabCPTs.length == 0) {
            LabTotalAmount = GrandTotal;


            $("#txtLabTotalAmount").setValue(GrandTotal);

            $("#txtLabTotal").empty();
            $("#txtLabTotal").append("Total Price = " + GrandTotal + "\tPKR");
            $("#txtTotalTest").empty();
            $("#txtTotalTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedLabCPTs.length + "");
           // $("#txtLabDiscountPer").trigger("onkeyup");// added by saqib
            $("#txtLabDiscountNet").trigger("onchange");
        }
    }
    $("#txtTotalTest").empty();
    $("#txtTotalTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedLabCPTs.length + "");

    $("#txtLabRefundBalance").setValue(0);
    @*if ('@ViewBag.IsRecieveAmount' == 'False' || $("#txtPatientAdmitId").getValue() != "")
        $("#txtLabPaidAmount").setValue(0);*@
}


   function LabPaymentModeChangeEvent() {
       debugger
       value = $("#ddl_LabPaymode").getValue();
       if (value != "") {
           if (PaymentModeList.length > 0 && $.isArray(PaymentModeList) != null) {
               var PaymentModeObject = $.grep(PaymentModeList, function (item) {
                   return item.ProfileId.toString() === value;
               })[0];
               if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PATPMD') {
                   $("#divLabPatientAdvance").show();
               }
               else {
                   $("#divLabPatientAdvance").hide();
               }
               if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PARPMD') {
                   $("#divLabCashReceived").show();
                   $("#divLabCreditCardReceived").show();
                   $("#divLabPatientAccountReceived").show();
                   $("#divLabPatientAdvance").show();
                   $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").disable();
                   let ReceivedAmmount = $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").getValue();

                   let CashReceived = $("#txtLabCashReceived").getValue();

                   if (CashReceived == "")
                       CashReceived = 0;
                   let CreditCardReceived = $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").getValue();
                   if (CreditCardReceived == "")
                       CreditCardReceived = 0;
                   let PatientAccountReceived = $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
                   if (PatientAccountReceived == "")
                       PatientAccountReceived = 0;
                   $("#txtLabCashReceived").setValue(ReceivedAmmount - CreditCardReceived - PatientAccountReceived);
                   $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").setValue(CreditCardReceived);
                   $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").setValue(PatientAccountReceived);


               }
               else {
                   $("#divLabCashReceived").hide();
                   $("#divLabCreditCardReceived").hide();
                   $("#divLabPatientAccountReceived").hide();
                   $("#txtLabCashReceived").setValue(0);
                   $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                   $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                   $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").enable();
                   if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PATPMD') {
                       $("#divLabPatientAdvance").show();
                   }
                   else {
                       $("#divLabPatientAdvance").hide();
                   }
               }
           }
       }
   }



   function LabHandlePaymentSelection(rowNo, serviceId, seviceObj, type) {


       var LabInsuranceCheckbox = document.getElementById("LabInsurance" + rowNo);
       var LabCashCheckbox = document.getElementById("LabCash" + rowNo);

       if (type === "insurance") {
           if (LabInsuranceCheckbox.checked) {
               LabCashCheckbox.checked = false; // Uncheck Cash if Insurance is checked
               LabRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
               var LabObjIns = new Object();
               LabObjIns.IndexNo = rowNo;
               LabObjIns.ServiceId = serviceId;
               LabObjIns.Quantity = $("#txtLabQuantity" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjIns.Instruction = $("#txtLabInstruction" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjIns.NORPRC = $("#txtLabModeInsPrice" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjIns.CopayPer = $("#txtLabCopayPercentage" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjIns.Copay = $("#txtLabCopay" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjIns.InsuranceDiscPer = $("#txtLabInsuranceDiscountPer" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjIns.InsuranceDiscAmount = $("#txtLabInsuranceDiscountPrice" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjIns.Deductible = $("#txtLabDeductible" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjIns.ApprovedPrice = $("#txtLabApprovedColumn" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjIns.RejectedPrice = $("#txtLabRejectedColumn" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjIns.IsInsuranceClaim = true;
               LabObjIns.PatientPrescribeLabTestId = seviceObj.PatientPrescribeLabTestId;
               LabObjIns.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId = seviceObj.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId;

               LabInsuranceArray.push(LabObjIns); // Add to Insurance array
           } else {
               LabRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
           }
       } else if (type === "cash") {
           if (LabCashCheckbox.checked) {
               LabInsuranceCheckbox.checked = false; // Uncheck Insurance if Cash is checked
               LabRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
               var LabObjCash = new Object();
               LabObjCash.IndexNo = rowNo;
               LabObjCash.ServiceId = serviceId;
               LabObjCash.Quantity = $("#txtLabQuantity" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjCash.Instruction = $("#txtLabInstruction" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjCash.NORPRC = $("#txtLabModePrice" + serviceId + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
               LabObjCash.IsInsuranceClaim = false;
               LabObjCash.PatientPrescribeLabTestId = seviceObj.PatientPrescribeLabTestId;
               LabObjCash.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId = seviceObj.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId;
               LabCashArray.push(LabObjCash); // Add to Cash array
           } else {
               LabRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo);
           }
       }
       LabUpdateInvoiceAmounts();
       CalculateGrandTotal();
   }


    function LabRemoveRowFromArrays(serviceId, rowNo) {

        LabCashArray = LabCashArray.filter(item => !(item.ServiceId == serviceId && item.IndexNo == rowNo));
        LabInsuranceArray = LabInsuranceArray.filter(item => !(item.ServiceId == serviceId && item.IndexNo == rowNo));


       //LabCashArray = LabCashArray.filter(item => item.ServiceId != serviceId);
       //LabInsuranceArray = LabInsuranceArray.filter(item => item.ServiceId != serviceId);
   }




   function LabUpdateInvoiceAmounts() {
       var cashTotal = LabCashArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.NORPRC * item.Quantity), 0);
       var insuranceTotal = LabInsuranceArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.NORPRC * item.Quantity), 0);
       var totalCopay = LabInsuranceArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + ((item.Copay * 1) + (item.Deductible * 1) + (item.RejectedPrice * 1)), 0);
       var totalTotalInsuranceDiscAmount = LabInsuranceArray.reduce((sum, item) => sum + ((item.InsuranceDiscAmount * 1)), 0);
       $("#txtLabTotalAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
       $("#txtLabPayableAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
       $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
       $("#txtLabPaidAmount").setValue(cashTotal);
       $("#txtLabBalance").setValue(0);
       $("#txtLabTotalRecievedAmount").setValue(cashTotal);

       $("#InsuranceLabtxtTotalAmount").setValue(insuranceTotal);
       $("#InsuranceLabTotalCopay").setValue(totalCopay.toFixed(2));
       $("#InsuranceLabtxtInsuranceDiscountAmount").setValue(totalTotalInsuranceDiscAmount.toFixed(2));
       $("#InsuranceLabtxtPayableByInsurance").setValue(insuranceTotal - totalTotalInsuranceDiscAmount - totalCopay);
       if (cashTotal == 0) {
           $("#txtLabDiscountNet").setValue(cashTotal);
       }
       $("#txtLabDiscountNet").trigger("change");


   }

   function LabfilterByCPCCode(val, e) {
       $(document).unbind("keydown");
       filteredCPTArray = new Array();
       $("#tblCPT").hide();
       $("#tblReferrals").hide();
       $("#tblReferralCodes").hide();
       $("#tblCPCCode").hide();
       if (val.trim() === "") {
           $("#tblCPCCode").hide();
           return;
       }
       //$("#tblReferrals").show();
       var dataw = filterArray(val, FilterGenderCPT);
       //filteredCPTArray = GetCPTFilterObjectArray(dataw);
       $("#tblCPCCode").show();
       var tbody = '';

       var tbody = '';
       tbody = GetCPTFilterTable(dataw);

       //if (e.keyCode == 13 && temp.length == 1) {
       //    searchByCode(temp[0].filterColumn);
       //}
       // SEARCHING PERFOME ON ENTER PRESS.
       if (e.keyCode == 13) {
           searchByCode(temp[0]);
       }

       //added by haroon 12/22/2014
       if (e.keyCode === 27) {
           $("#tblCPCCode").hide();

       }
       //end
       if (tbody.trim() == '') {
           $("#tblCPCCode").hide();
           $(document).unbind("keydown");
       }
       else {
           BindTblCPTArrowKeys("tblCPCCode", "txtCPTCode", "searchByCode");
       }

       $("#tblCPCCode").html(tbody);
   }


   function CalculateLabNetDiscount(val) {
       debugger
       /* var price = $("#txtLabTotalAmount").getValue();*/
       LabChangePrice = "True";
       var price = GetLabTotalPrice();
       $("#txtLabTotalAmount").setValue(price);
       var balance = $("#txtLabBalance").getValue();

       var disc = new Number(val);
       var paid = Math.floor(price - disc);
       //if (locationType == LOC_LABORATORY && patientType != PATTYPE_COMPANY)
       //    if (!ValidateDiscount(price, allowedDiscount, "net", disc)) {
       //        $("#txtLabDiscountNet").focus();
       //        return;
       //    }


       if (price < disc) {
           ShowMessage('1', "You can maximum give discount Rs." + Math.floor(new Number(price)));
           $("#txtLabDiscountNet").focus();
           validDiscount = false;
           return;
       }

       var perDisc = (disc / price) * 100;


       if (isNaN(perDisc)) {
           $("#txtLabDiscountPer").setValue(0);
       }
       else {
           $("#txtLabDiscountPer").setValue(new Number(perDisc).toFixed(2));
       }


       let CashReceived = $("#txtLabCashReceived").getValue();

       if (CashReceived == "")
           CashReceived = 0;
       let CreditCardReceived = $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").getValue();
       if (CreditCardReceived == "")
           CreditCardReceived = 0;
       let PatientAccountReceived = $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
       if (PatientAccountReceived == "")
           PatientAccountReceived = 0;

       $("#txtLabPayableAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - disc));
       $("#txtLabPaidAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - disc));
       $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - disc));
       debugger
       value = $("#ddl_LabPaymode").getValue();
       if (value != "") {
           if (PaymentModeList.length > 0 && $.isArray(PaymentModeList) != null) {
               var PaymentModeObject = $.grep(PaymentModeList, function (item) {
                   return item.ProfileId.toString() === value;
               })[0];
               if (LabChangePrice == "True") {
                   if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PARPMD') {
                       $("#txtLabCashReceived").setValue(price - disc);
                       $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                       $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                   }
                   else {
                       $("#txtLabCashReceived").setValue(0);
                       $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                       $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                   }
                   LabChangePrice = "False";
               }
               else {
                   if (PaymentModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PARPMD') {

                       $("#txtLabCashReceived").setValue(Math.floor(price - CreditCardReceived - PatientAccountReceived - disAmount));
                       $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").setValue(CreditCardReceived);
                       $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").setValue(PatientAccountReceived);
                   }
                   else {
                       $("#txtLabCashReceived").setValue(0);
                       $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
                       $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
                   }
               }
           }
       }

       $("#txtLabTotalRecievedAmount").setValue($("#txtLabPayableAmount").val());

       CalculateLabRemainingAmount();


   }
   function GetLabTotalPrice() {
       debugger
       var getTotalPrice = 0;
       //var getInsuraceTotalPrice = 0
       try {
           if (LabCashArray != null) {
               for (var i = 0; i < LabCashArray.length; i++) {
                   var getPrice = $("#txtLabModePrice" + LabCashArray[i].ServiceId + "_" + LabCashArray[i].IndexNo).getValue();
                   //if (LabCashArray[i].InsuranceClaimStatus == 2) {
                   //    if (getPrice == "")
                   //        getPrice = 0;
                   //    getInsuraceTotalPrice = new Number(getInsuraceTotalPrice) + new Number(getPrice);
                   //}

                   if (getPrice == "")
                       getPrice = 0;
                   getTotalPrice = new Number(getTotalPrice) + new Number(getPrice);


               }
               //$("#txtPayableByInsurance").setValue(getInsuraceTotalPrice);
           }
           return getTotalPrice;
       } catch (e) {
           console.log(e.message);
       }
   }
   function CalculateLabPerDiscount(val) {
       //var price = $("#txtLabTotalAmount").getValue();


       var price = GetLabTotalPrice();
       /*var price = 0;*/
       $("#txtLabTotalAmount").setValue(price);


       var balance = $("#txtLabBalance").getValue();


       var disc = new Number(val);
       var disAmount = Math.round((price / 100) * disc);
       var paid = Math.floor(price - disAmount);
       var dis = $("#txtLabDiscountNet").getValue();
       //if (locationType == LOC_LABORATORY && patientType != PATTYPE_COMPANY)
       //    if (!ValidateDiscount(price, allowedDiscount, "per", disc)) {
       //        $("#txtLabDiscountPer").focus();
       //        return;
       //    }

       if (disc > 100) {
           ShowMessage('1', "Invalid discount");
           $("#txtLabDiscountPer").focus();
           validDiscount = false;
           return;
       }
       $("#txtLabPayableAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - dis));
       $("#txtLabPaidAmount").setValue(Math.floor(price - dis));
       $("#txtLabCashReceived").setValue(Math.floor(price - dis));
       $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").setValue(0);
       $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").setValue(0);
       @*if ('@ViewBag.labId' != '') // saqib
           $("#txtLabReceived").setValue(Math.floor(price - disAmount)); // saqib discount*@
       $("#txtLabTotalRecievedAmount").setValue($("#txtLabReceived").val()); // saqib discount


       //var netDisc = (val / 100) * price;

       //$("#txtLabDiscountNet").setValue(Math.round(netDisc));

       CalculateLabRemainingAmount();

   }
   function CalculateLabCurrentRemainingAmount() {
       var currentrecived = $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").getValue();
       var payedAmount = $("#txtLabPaidAmount").getValue();
       var payAbleAmount = $("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue();
       var netRecieved = $("#txtLabReceived").getValue();

       var dueRecived = $("#txtLabDueRecieved").getValue();


       var balanceAmount = new Number(netRecieved) + new Number(currentrecived) - new Number(dueRecived);
       balanceAmount = (new Number($("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue())) - (new Number($("#txtLabReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabCurrentAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabReturn").getValue()));//new Number(payAbleAmount) - balanceAmount;

       if (balanceAmount < 0) {
           ShowMessage('1', MSG_BALANCE);
           $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").setValue(0);
           $("#txtLabPaidAmount").setValue(0);

           $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").focus();
           $("#txtLabBalance").setValue((new Number($("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue())) - (new Number($("#txtLabReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabCurrentAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabReturn").getValue())));

           return false;
       }
       var totalRecievedAmount = new Number(netRecieved) + new Number(currentrecived);
       $("#txtLabBalance").setValue(new Number($("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue()) - (new Number($("#txtLabTotalRecievedAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabCurrentAmount").getValue())));

       $("#txtLabPaidAmount").setValue(new Number($("#txtLabReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabCurrentAmount").getValue()));
       $("#txtLabTotalRecievedAmount").setValue(new Number($("#txtLabReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabDueRecieved").getValue()));
       $("#txtLabBalance").setValue((new Number($("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue())) - (new Number($("#txtLabReceived").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabDueRecieved").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabCurrentAmount").getValue()) + new Number($("#txtLabReturn").getValue())));

       return true;
   }
   function CalculateLabParitalReceivedAmount() {
       debugger
       $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").setValue(0);
       var CashAmount = $("#txtLabCashReceived").getValue();
       var CreditAmount = $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").getValue();
       var PatientAmount = $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
       var LabTotalAmount = new Number(CashAmount) + new Number(CreditAmount) + new Number(PatientAmount);
       $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").setValue(LabTotalAmount);
       CalculateLabCurrentRemainingAmount();
   }
   function CalculateLabRemainingAmount() {
       debugger
       var payedAmount = $("#txtLabPaidAmount").getValue();
       var payAbleAmount = $("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue();
       var netRecieved = $("#txtLabReceived").getValue();
       var dueRecieved = $("#txtLabDueRecieved").getValue();


       var currentRecived = new Number($("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue()) - new Number($("#txtLabTotalRecievedAmount").getValue());


       debugger
       var balanceAmount = new Number($("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue()) - (new Number($("#txtLabTotalRecievedAmount").getValue()));
       $("#txtLabPaidAmount").setValue(new Number($("#txtLabTotalRecievedAmount").getValue()));
       if (balanceAmount < 0) {
           ShowMessage('1', MSG_BALANCE);
           $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").setValue(0);
           $("#txtLabPaidAmount").setValue(0);
           $("#txtLabCurrentAmount").focus();
           return false;
       }

       $("#txtLabBalance").setValue(balanceAmount);

       return true;
   }



    function LabCalculateRejectedPrice(rowNo, id, obj, price, e) {

        let insuranceGrossPrice = $("#txtLabModeInsPrice" + id + "_" + rowNo).getValue();
        let CopayPer = $("#txtLabCopayPercentage" + id + "_" + rowNo).getValue();

        let rejectedPrice = (insuranceGrossPrice - price).toFixed(2);
        $("#txtLabRejectedColumn" + id + "_" + rowNo).setValue(rejectedPrice);
        LabCalculateCopayAmount(rowNo, id, obj, CopayPer);

        for (var j = 0; j < selectedLabCPTs.length; j++) {
            if (id == selectedLabCPTs[j].ServiceId) {

                selectedLabCPTs[j].RejectedPrice = parseFloat(rejectedPrice);
                break;

            }

        }

    }

    function LabCalculateDeductiblePrice(rowNo, id, obj, price, e) {
        $("#LabInsurance" + rowNo).prop("checked", true);
        LabHandlePaymentSelection(rowNo, id, obj, "insurance");
    }


    function LabCalculateCopayAmount(rowNo, id, obj, CopayPer, e) {

        let insuranceGrossPrice = $("#txtLabApprovedColumn" + id + "_" + rowNo).getValue();

        let Copay = 0
        if (!isNaN(CopayPer) && CopayPer > 0) {
            Copay = (insuranceGrossPrice / 100) * CopayPer;
            Copay = Copay.toFixed(2);
        } else {
            Copay = 0; // fallback value or you can set to null or a default percentage
        }

        $("#txtLabCopay" + id + "_" + rowNo).setValue(Copay);

        for (var j = 0; j < selectedLabCPTs.length; j++) {
            if (id == selectedLabCPTs[j].ServiceId) {

                selectedLabCPTs[j].Copay = parseFloat(Copay);
                break;

            }

        }

        $("#LabInsurance" + rowNo).prop("checked", true);
        LabHandlePaymentSelection(rowNo, id, obj, "insurance");
    }



   function LabChangePriceMode(id, price, e) {
       var priceMode = "NORPRC";
       LabTotalAmount = 0;
       LabChangePrice = "True";
       var found = false;
       for (var j = 0; j < selectedLabCPTs.length; j++) {
           if (id == selectedLabCPTs[j].ServiceId) {


               selectedLabCPTs[j].ServicePriceModePrefix = "NORPRC";
               selectedLabCPTs[j].Price = price;
               selectedLabCPTs[j].NORPRC = price;
               selectedLabCPTs[j].PriceForEdit = price;

               for (var k = 0; k < lstPriceMode.length; k++) {
                   if (lstPriceMode[k].ProfilePrefix == priceMode) {
                       selectedLabCPTs[j].ServicePriceModeId = lstPriceMode[k].ProfileId;
                   }
               }
           }
           if (selectedLabCPTs[j].Price != undefined) {
               LabTotalAmount = new Number(LabTotalAmount) + new Number(selectedLabCPTs[j].Price);
           }
       }
       LabTotalAmount = GetLabTotalPrice();
       //LabTotalAmount = 0;
       if (LabTotalAmount != 0) {
           $("#txtLabTotalAmount").setValue(LabTotalAmount);
           $("#txtLabPayableAmount").setValue(LabTotalAmount);
           $("#txtLabBalance").setValue(LabTotalAmount);
           // $("#txtLabPaidAmount").setValue(LabTotalAmount); //saqib

           $("#txtLabTotal").empty();
           $("#txtLabTotal").append("Total Price = " + LabTotalAmount + "\tPKR");
           $("#txtTotalTest").empty();
           $("#txtTotalTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedLabCPTs.length + "");
           $("#txtLabDiscountNet").trigger("onchange");

           //CalculateLabPerDiscount($("#txtLabDiscountPer").getValue());

       }
       $("#txtTotalTest").empty();
       $("#txtTotalTest").append("Total Test = " + selectedLabCPTs.length + "");
   }



   function GetLabInvoiceObjCash() {

       try {
           var objVoucher = new Object();
           objVoucher.PayModeProfileId = $("#ddl_LabPaymode").getValue();
           var objInvoice = new Object();

           objInvoice.InvoiceId = $("#txtLabInvoiceId").getValue();
           objInvoice.VoucherId = $("#txtLabVoucherId").getValue();
           objInvoice.ReceiptVoucherId = $("#txtLabReceiptVoucherId").getValue();
           objInvoice.CashReceived = $("#txtLabCashReceived").getValue();
           objInvoice.CreditCardReceived = $("#txtLabCreditCardReceived").getValue();
           objInvoice.PatientAccountReceived = $("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").getValue();
           objInvoice.TotalReceived = $("#txtLabPaidAmount").getValue();

           objVoucher.VoucherId = $("#txtLabVoucherReceiptId").getValue();
           objVoucher.TotalCredit = objInvoice.TotalReceived;
           objVoucher.TotalDebit = objInvoice.TotalReceived;

           objInvoice.Voucher1 = objVoucher;

           return objInvoice;
       } catch (e) {

       }

   }

   function GetLabCashOrderDetailObj() {
       var LabTotalAmount = $("#txtLabTotalAmount").getValue();
       var discountNet = $("#txtLabDiscountNet").getValue();
       var discPer = $("#txtLabDiscountPer").getValue();
       var payAmount = $("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue();

       var payMode = $("#ddl_LabPaymode").getValue();

       var paidAmount = $("#txtLabPaidAmount").getValue();
       var balance = $("#txtLabBalance").getValue();
       var miscAmount = 0;
       var tax = 0;

       let profilePrefix = "";

       var ServicePackageId = 0;
       var lstCashOrderDetail = new Array();

       var lineID = 1;

       for (var i = 0; i < LabCashArray.length; i++) {
           debugger
           var cpcDiscount = 0;
           var grossAmount = 0;
           var amount = 0;

           var objCashOrdDetail = new Object();
           if (LabCashArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId != null) {
               objCashOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = LabCashArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
           }
           objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailSet = new Object();
           if (LabCashArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId != undefined) {
               objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = LabCashArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId;

           }
           else {
               objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = 0;
           }

           if (profilePrefix != "GRTPAT") {
               if (LabCashArray[i].ServicePackageId == undefined) {
                   if (objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                       if (LabCashArray[i].PriceForEdit == 0) {
                           ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                           return;
                       }
                   }
                   else {
                       if (LabCashArray[i].NORPRC != undefined)
                           if (LabCashArray[i].NORPRC == 0) {
                               ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                               return;
                           }
                   }
               }
           }

           objCashOrdDetail.DiscPercent = discPer;

           if (LabCashArray[i].ServicePackageId != undefined) {
               ServicePackageId = LabCashArray[i].ServicePackageId;
               objCashOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = LabCashArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
           }
           objCashOrdDetail.PriceModeProfileId = LabCashArray[i].ServicePriceModeId;

           objCashOrdDetail.ServiceId = LabCashArray[i].ServiceId
           objCashOrdDetail.PatientPrescribeLabTestId = LabCashArray[i].PatientPrescribeLabTestId;
           objCashOrdDetail.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId = LabCashArray[i].PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId;

           if (LabCashArray[i].IsSTAT) {
               cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(LabTotalAmount, LabCashArray[i].STATPrice, discountNet);
               grossAmount = new Number(LabCashArray[i].STATPrice) - new Number(cpcDiscount);
               amount = LabCashArray[i].STATPrice;
           }
           else {
               if (objCashOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                   cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(LabTotalAmount, LabCashArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                   grossAmount = new Number(LabCashArray[i].NORPRC) - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                   amount = LabCashArray[i].NORPRC;
               }
               else {
                   cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(LabTotalAmount, LabCashArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                   grossAmount = new Number(LabCashArray[i].NORPRC) - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                   amount = LabCashArray[i].NORPRC;
               }


           }
           objCashOrdDetail.IsInsuranceClaim = LabCashArray[i].IsInsuranceClaim;
           objCashOrdDetail.Amount = amount;
           objCashOrdDetail.Price = amount;
           objCashOrdDetail.Quantity = LabCashArray[i].Quantity || 1;
           //objCashOrdDetail.Quantity = Quantity;
           objCashOrdDetail.DiscPerUnit = cpcDiscount;
           objCashOrdDetail.DiscountAmount = cpcDiscount;
           objCashOrdDetail.GrossAmount = grossAmount;

           objCashOrdDetail.MiscPerUnit = 0;
           objCashOrdDetail.MiscAmount = 0;
           objCashOrdDetail.NetAmount = grossAmount;
           objCashOrdDetail.NetPrice = grossAmount;
           objCashOrdDetail.ReceivableAmount = grossAmount;
           objCashOrdDetail.TaxAmount = 0;
           objCashOrdDetail.TaxPercent = 0;
           objCashOrdDetail.LineDescription = LabCashArray[i].Remarks;

           objCashOrdDetail.ReportDateTime = LabCashArray[i].ReportDateTime;
           objCashOrdDetail.IsSampleBrought = LabCashArray[i].IsSampleBrought;
           lstCashOrderDetail.push(objCashOrdDetail);
           lineID++;
       }

       return lstCashOrderDetail;
   }

   function GetLabINSOrderDetailObj() {

       let profilePrefix = "";

       var ServicePackageId = 0;
       let discountNet = 0;
       let LabTotalAmount = $("#InsuranceLabtxtTotalAmount").getValue();
       var lstInsOrderDetail = new Array();
       let lineID = 1;
       for (var i = 0; i < LabInsuranceArray.length; i++) {
           debugger
           var cpcDiscount = 0;
           var grossAmount = 0;
           var amount = 0;
           var objINSOrdDetail = new Object();
           if (LabInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId != null) {
               objINSOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = LabInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
           }
           objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailSet = new Object();
           if (LabInsuranceArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId != undefined) {
               objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = LabInsuranceArray[i].PatientOrderDetailId;
           }
           else {
               objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId = 0;
           }
           if (profilePrefix != "GRTPAT") {
               if (LabInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageId == undefined) {
                   if (objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                       if (LabInsuranceArray[i].PriceForEdit == 0) {
                           ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                           return;
                       }
                   }
                   else {
                       if (LabInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC != undefined)
                           if (LabInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC == 0) {
                               ShowMessage(1, "Please Add Test Price First");
                               return;
                           }
                   }
               }
           }

           objINSOrdDetail.DiscPercent = 0;
           if (LabInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageId != undefined) {
               ServicePackageId = LabInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageId;
               objINSOrdDetail.ServicePackageDetailId = LabInsuranceArray[i].ServicePackageDetailId;
           }
           objINSOrdDetail.PriceModeProfileId = LabInsuranceArray[i].ServicePriceModeId;

           objINSOrdDetail.ServiceId = LabInsuranceArray[i].ServiceId
           objINSOrdDetail.PatientPrescribeLabTestId = LabInsuranceArray[i].PatientPrescribeLabTestId;
           objINSOrdDetail.PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId = LabInsuranceArray[i].PatientDischargeSummaryLabTestId;

           if (LabInsuranceArray[i].IsSTAT) {
               cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(LabTotalAmount, LabInsuranceArray[i].STATPrice, discountNet);
               grossAmount = new Number(LabInsuranceArray[i].STATPrice); //- new Number(cpcDiscount);
               amount = LabInsuranceArray[i].STATPrice;
           }
           else {
               if (objINSOrdDetail.PatientOrderDetailId != 0) {
                   cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(LabTotalAmount, LabInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                   grossAmount = new Number(LabInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC);// - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                   amount = LabInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC;
               }
               else {
                   cpcDiscount = CalculateCPCDiscount(LabTotalAmount, LabInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC, discountNet);
                   grossAmount = new Number(LabInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC);// - new Number(cpcDiscount);
                   amount = LabInsuranceArray[i].NORPRC;
               }
           }



           objINSOrdDetail.IsInsuranceClaim = LabInsuranceArray[i].IsInsuranceClaim;
           objINSOrdDetail.Amount = amount;
           objINSOrdDetail.Price = (LabInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (LabInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (LabInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
           objINSOrdDetail.Copay = LabInsuranceArray[i].Copay;
           objINSOrdDetail.CopayPer = LabInsuranceArray[i].CopayPer;
           objINSOrdDetail.Deductible = LabInsuranceArray[i].Deductible;
           objINSOrdDetail.ApprovedPrice = LabInsuranceArray[i].ApprovedPrice;
           objINSOrdDetail.RejectedPrice = LabInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice;
           objINSOrdDetail.InsuranceDiscPer = LabInsuranceArray[i].InsuranceDiscPer;
           objINSOrdDetail.InsuranceDiscAmount = LabInsuranceArray[i].InsuranceDiscAmount;
           objINSOrdDetail.Quantity = LabInsuranceArray[i].Quantity || 1;
           objINSOrdDetail.DiscPerUnit = cpcDiscount;
           objINSOrdDetail.DiscountAmount = 0;
           objINSOrdDetail.GrossAmount = 0;
           objINSOrdDetail.MiscPerUnit = 0;
           objINSOrdDetail.MiscAmount = 0;
           objINSOrdDetail.NetAmount = (LabInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (LabInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (LabInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
           objINSOrdDetail.NetPrice = (LabInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (LabInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (LabInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
           objINSOrdDetail.ReceivableAmount = (LabInsuranceArray[i].Copay * 1) + (LabInsuranceArray[i].Deductible * 1) + (LabInsuranceArray[i].RejectedPrice * 1);
           objINSOrdDetail.TaxAmount = 0;
           objINSOrdDetail.TaxPercent = 0;
           objINSOrdDetail.LineDescription = LabInsuranceArray[i].Remarks;
           objINSOrdDetail.ReportDateTime = LabInsuranceArray[i].ReportDateTime;
           objINSOrdDetail.IsSampleBrought = LabInsuranceArray[i].IsSampleBrought;
           lstInsOrderDetail.push(objINSOrdDetail);
           lineID++;
       }

       return lstInsOrderDetail;
   }

   }


   function SaveLabObj() {
   debugger
       var patientCat = $("#ddl_PatientCategory").getValue();


       value = $("#ddl_LabPaymode").getValue();
       if (PaymentModeList.length > 0 && $.isArray(PaymentModeList) != null && LabCashArray.length > 0) {
           // Use $.grep to find the object with the specified ID
           var PayModeObject = $.grep(PaymentModeList, function (item) {
               return item.ProfileId.toString() === value;
           })[0];
           debugger
           if (PayModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PATPMD') {

               let PatientRecieveAmount = parseInt($("#txtLabPaidAmount").getValue());
               let PatientAdvance = $("#txtLabPatientAdvance").getValue();
               if (PatientAdvance == "") {
                   PatientAdvance = 0;
               }
               PatientAdvance = parseInt(PatientAdvance);

               if (PatientRecieveAmount > PatientAdvance) {
                   ShowMessage('1', "Patient has low balance in Patient Account");
                   return;
               }

           }
           else if (PayModeObject.ProfilePrefix == 'PARPMD') {

               let PatientPayablePatientAccount = parseInt($("#txtLabPatientAccountReceived").getValue());
               //PatientPayable = new Number(PatientPayable) ;
               let PatientAdvance = $("#txtLabPatientAdvance").getValue();
               if (PatientAdvance == "") {
                   PatientAdvance = 0;
               }
               PatientAdvance = parseInt(PatientAdvance);

               //PatientAdvance = new Number(PatientAdvance);


               if (PatientPayablePatientAccount > PatientAdvance) {
                   ShowMessage('1', "Patient has low balance in Patient Account");
                   return;
               }

           }
       }
       let listobj = new Array();
       //if (ProCashArray.length > 0) {
       //    debugger
       //    let CashObj = GetProPatientOrderObjForCash();
       //    listobj.push(CashObj);
       //    if (!CalculateProRemainingAmount()) {
       //        return;
       //    }
       //}
       //if (ProInsuranceArray.length > 0) {
       //    let InsuranceObj = GetProPatientOrderObjForInsurance();
       //    listobj.push(InsuranceObj);
       //}

       if (LabCashArray.length > 0) {
           debugger
           let CashObj = GetLabPatientOrderObjForCash();
           listobj.push(CashObj);
           if (!CalculateLabRemainingAmount()) {
               return;
           }
       }
       if (LabInsuranceArray.length > 0) {
           let InsuranceObj = GetLabPatientOrderObjForInsurance();
           listobj.push(InsuranceObj);
       }


       //if (RadCashArray.length > 0) {
       //    debugger
       //    let CashObj = GetRadPatientOrderObjForCash();
       //    listobj.push(CashObj);
       //    if (!CalculateRadRemainingAmount()) {
       //        return;
       //    }
       //}
       //if (RadInsuranceArray.length > 0) {
       //    let InsuranceObj = GetRadPatientOrderObjForInsurance();
       //    listobj.push(InsuranceObj);
       //}


   if (!listobj || listobj.length === 0) {
       ShowMessage(1, "Please Select Test");
       return;
   }

       var obj = new Object();
       obj.PatientOrders = listobj;

   function GetLabPatientOrderObjForCash() {
       debugger
       let LabTotalAmount = $("#txtLabTotalAmount").getValue();
       let discountNet = $("#txtLabDiscountNet").getValue();
       let discPer = $("#txtLabDiscountPer").getValue();
       let payAmount = $("#txtLabPayableAmount").getValue();


       let paidAmount = $("#txtLabPaidAmount").getValue();
       let balance = $("#txtLabBalance").getValue();
       let miscAmount = 0;
       let tax = 0;
       let cashObj = new Object();
       cashObj = GetPatientOrderObjData();
       cashObj.DocMovement = new Object();
       cashObj.DocMovement.ShortName = 'LIMPOD';

       cashObj.PatientOrderSet.RefPersonName = $("#txtDepartmentComponentId option:selected").text();
       cashObj.PatientOrderSet.PaymentMethodProfileId = $("#ddl_LabPaymode").getValue();
       cashObj.PatientOrderSet.PatientOrderSetId = $("#txtLabPatientOrderSetId").getValue();
       cashObj.PatientOrderId = $("#txtLabPatientOrderId").getValue();

       cashObj.InvoiceId = $("#txtLabInvoiceId").getValue();
       cashObj.PatientOrderSet.IsInsuranceOrder = false;
       cashObj.TotalAmount = Math.floor(LabTotalAmount);
       cashObj.TotalAmountDecimal = LabTotalAmount
       cashObj.TotalDiscount = discountNet;
       cashObj.TotalGross = payAmount;
       cashObj.TotalMisc = miscAmount;
       cashObj.TotalNet = payAmount;
       cashObj.TotalReceivable = payAmount;
       cashObj.TotalTax = tax;
       cashObj.DiscPercent = discPer;
       cashObj.Patient = new Object();
       cashObj.Patient = GetPatientObjData();
       cashObj.PatientOrderDetails = new Array();
       cashObj.PatientOrderDetails = GetLabCashOrderDetailObj();
       cashObj.Invoice = new Object();
       cashObj.Invoice = GetLabInvoiceObjCash();

       return cashObj;
   }



   function GetLabPatientOrderObjForInsurance() {

       debugger



       let LabInsurancetotalAmount = $("#InsuranceLabtxtTotalAmount").getValue();
       let totalCopay = $("#InsuranceLabTotalCopay").getValue();
       let PayablebyInsurance = $("#InsuranceLabtxtPayableByInsurance").getValue();
       let insuranceDiscountAmount = $("#InsuranceLabtxtInsuranceDiscountAmount").getValue();

       let INSObj = new Object();
       INSObj = GetPatientOrderObjData();
       INSObj.DocMovement = new Object();
       INSObj.DocMovement.ShortName = 'LIMPOD';

       INSObj.PatientOrderSet.RefPersonName = $("#txtDepartmentComponentId option:selected").text();
       INSObj.PatientOrderSet.PaymentMethodProfileId = $("#ddl_InsuranceLabPaymode").getValue();
       INSObj.PatientOrderSet.PatientOrderSetId = $("#txtLabInsPatientOrderSetId").getValue();
       INSObj.PatientOrderId = $("#txtLabInsPatientOrderId").getValue();
       INSObj.PatientOrderSet.IsInsuranceOrder = true;
       INSObj.TotalAmount = Math.floor(LabInsurancetotalAmount);
       INSObj.TotalAmountDecimal = LabInsurancetotalAmount;
       INSObj.TotalCopay = totalCopay;
       INSObj.TotalDiscount = 0;
       INSObj.TotalGross = (totalCopay * 1);
       INSObj.TotalMisc = 0;
       INSObj.TotalNet = 0;
       INSObj.TotalReceivable = (totalCopay * 1);

       INSObj.PayableToInsurance = PayablebyInsurance;
       INSObj.InsuranceDiscountAmount = insuranceDiscountAmount;
       INSObj.TotalTax = 0;

       INSObj.Patient = new Object();
       INSObj.Patient = GetPatientObjData();

       INSObj.PatientOrderDetails = new Array();
       INSObj.PatientOrderDetails = GetLabINSOrderDetailObj();
       INSObj.Invoice = new Object();
       INSObj.Invoice = GetLabInsInvoiceObjCash();


       return INSObj;

   }

</script>
